You are a security expert and consistency reviewer performing a second-round code review of a Python-to-TypeScript migration. The project is memorytree-workflow at D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow, branch ts.

Focus on these specific areas:

1. Security review:
- SQL injection in src/transcript/db.ts — are parameters properly bound?
- Command injection in src/utils/exec.ts — is execFileSync safe?
- Path traversal in import/discover/scaffold — can user input escape intended directories?
- Sensitive data in logs — does log.ts or heartbeat.ts leak secrets?
- Lock file race conditions in lock.ts — TOCTOU issues?

2. Cross-module consistency:
- Do all modules use toPosixPath consistently for persistent writes?
- Is normalizeTimestamp used consistently across heartbeat, import, alert?
- Are ManifestEntry fields consistent between import.ts, db.ts, and types/transcript.ts?
- Does the barrel export in transcript/index.ts expose everything needed?

3. Test coverage gaps:
- Read ALL test files in tests/. Identify functions that lack test coverage.
- Check edge cases: empty inputs, Unicode, Windows paths, concurrent access
- Verify test isolation (temp dirs cleaned up, no global state leaks)

4. API contract:
- Does the CLI output match the Python CLI output format? (JSON keys, field names)
- Are all commander options registered correctly in main.ts?
- Does SKILL.md reference any remaining Python paths?

Read ALL relevant files. Give specific file:line references. Rate issues as CRITICAL / HIGH / MEDIUM / LOW.

1→/**
     2→ * Transcript search index — SQLite upsert for the global transcript catalog.
     3→ *
     4→ * Uses sql.js (WebAssembly SQLite) so the module works without a native
     5→ * sqlite3 binding.  The WASM init is async; we cache the resulting factory
     6→ * promise so it is only resolved once per process.
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import initSqlJs, { type SqlJsStatic } from 'sql.js'
    10→import { existsSync, readFileSync, writeFileSync } from 'node:fs'
    11→import type { ManifestEntry } from '../types/transcript.js'
    12→
    13→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    14→// Lazy sql.js initialisation (cached promise)
    15→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    16→
    17→let sqlPromise: Promise<SqlJsStatic> | null = null
    18→
    19→function getSqlJs(): Promise<SqlJsStatic> {
    20→  if (sqlPromise === null) {
    21→    sqlPromise = initSqlJs()
    22→  }
    23→  return sqlPromise
    24→}
    25→
    26→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    27→// Column definitions
    28→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    29→
    30→const PK_COLUMNS = [
    31→  'client',
    32→  'project',
    33→  'session_id',
    34→  'raw_sha256',
    35→] as const
    36→
    37→const DATA_COLUMNS = [
    38→  'title',
    39→  'started_at',
    40→  'imported_at',
    41→  'cwd',
    42→  'branch',
    43→  'raw_source_path',
    44→  'raw_upload_permission',
    45→  'global_raw_path',
    46→  'global_clean_path',
    47→  'repo_raw_path',
    48→  'repo_clean_path',
    49→  'repo_manifest_path',
    50→  'message_count',
    51→  'tool_event_count',
    52→] as const
    53→
    54→const ALL_COLUMNS = [...PK_COLUMNS, ...DATA_COLUMNS] as const
    55→
    56→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    57→// SQL statements (built once)
    58→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    59→
    60→const CREATE_TABLE_SQL = `
    61→  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS transcripts (
    62→    client              TEXT    NOT NULL,
    63→    project             TEXT    NOT NULL,
    64→    session_id          TEXT    NOT NULL,
    65→    raw_sha256          TEXT    NOT NULL,
    66→    title               TEXT    NOT NULL,
    67→    started_at          TEXT    NOT NULL,
    68→    imported_at         TEXT    NOT NULL,
    69→    cwd                 TEXT    NOT NULL,
    70→    branch              TEXT    NOT NULL,
    71→    raw_source_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
    72→    raw_upload_permission TEXT  NOT NULL,
    73→    global_raw_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
    74→    global_clean_path   TEXT    NOT NULL,
    75→    repo_raw_path       TEXT    NOT NULL,
    76→    repo_clean_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
    77→    repo_manifest_path  TEXT    NOT NULL,
    78→    message_count       INTEGER NOT NULL,
    79→    tool_event_count    INTEGER NOT NULL,
    80→    PRIMARY KEY (client, project, session_id, raw_sha256)
    81→  )
    82→`
    83→
    84→const UPSERT_SQL = `
    85→  INSERT INTO transcripts (
    86→    ${ALL_COLUMNS.join(', ')}
    87→  ) VALUES (${ALL_COLUMNS.map(() => '?').join(', ')})
    88→  ON CONFLICT(${PK_COLUMNS.join(', ')}) DO UPDATE SET
    89→    ${DATA_COLUMNS.map((c) => `${c} = excluded.${c}`).join(',\n    ')}
    90→`
    91→
    92→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    93→// Public API
    94→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    95→
    96→/**
    97→ * Insert or update a single transcript manifest row in the SQLite search
    98→ * index at `dbPath`.  Creates the database and table if they do not exist.
    99→ *
   100→ * The function is async because the first call must initialise the sql.js
   101→ * WASM module.
   102→ */
   103→export async function upsertSearchIndex(
   104→  dbPath: string,
   105→  manifest: ManifestEntry,
   106→): Promise<void> {
   107→  const SQL = await getSqlJs()
   108→
   109→  const db = existsSync(dbPath)
   110→    ? new SQL.Database(readFileSync(dbPath))
   111→    : new SQL.Database()
   112→
   113→  try {
   114→    db.run('PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL')
   115→    db.run(CREATE_TABLE_SQL)
   116→
   117→    const record: Record<string, unknown> = { ...manifest }
   118→    const params = ALL_COLUMNS.map((col) => {
   119→      const value = record[col]
   120→      if (value === undefined || value === null) {
   121→        return ''
   122→      }
   123→      return typeof value === 'number' ? value : String(value)
   124→    })
   125→
   126→    db.run(UPSERT_SQL, params)
   127→
   128→    const data = db.export()
   129→    writeFileSync(dbPath, Buffer.from(data))
   130→  } finally {
   131→    db.close()
   132→  }
   133→}
   134→

Read output=1→/** 2→ * MemoryTree heartbeat — single execution, stateless, idempotent. 3→ * Port of scripts/heartbeat.py 4→ */ 5→ 6→import type { ParsedTranscript } from '../types/transcrip...
Show output payload 
1→/**
     2→ * MemoryTree heartbeat — single execution, stateless, idempotent.
     3→ * Port of scripts/heartbeat.py
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import type { ParsedTranscript } from '../types/transcript.js'
     7→import { discoverSourceFiles, transcriptMatchesRepo } from '../transcript/discover.js'
     8→import { importTranscript, transcriptHasContent } from '../transcript/import.js'
     9→import { parseTranscript } from '../transcript/parse.js'
    10→import { slugify } from '../transcript/common.js'
    11→import { defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot } from '../transcript/discover.js'
    12→import type { Config } from './config.js'
    13→import { loadConfig } from './config.js'
    14→import { acquireLock, releaseLock } from './lock.js'
    15→import { resetFailureCount, writeAlert, writeAlertWithThreshold } from './alert.js'
    16→import type { LogLevel } from './log.js'
    17→import { getLogger, setupLogging } from './log.js'
    18→import { git } from '../utils/exec.js'
    19→import { toPosixPath } from '../utils/path.js'
    20→import { resolve } from 'node:path'
    21→import { existsSync } from 'node:fs'
    22→
    23→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    24→// Sensitive pattern detection
    25→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    26→
    27→const SENSITIVE_PATTERNS: readonly RegExp[] = [
    28→  /(?:api[_-]?key|apikey)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,
    29→  /(?:password|passwd|pwd)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,
    30→  /(?:secret|token)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,
    31→  /(?:sk-|pk_live_|sk_live_|ghp_|gho_|glpat-)\S{10,}/,
    32→  /Bearer\s+\S{20,}/i,
    33→]
    34→
    35→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    36→// Main entry point
    37→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    38→
    39→export async function main(): Promise<number> {
    40→  const config = loadConfig()
    41→  setupLogging(config.log_level as LogLevel)
    42→  const logger = getLogger()
    43→
    44→  if (!acquireLock()) {
    45→    logger.info('Another heartbeat instance is running. Exiting.')
    46→    writeAlert('global', 'lock_held', 'Heartbeat exited: another instance held the lock.')
    47→    return 0
    48→  }
    49→
    50→  try {
    51→    return await runHeartbeat(config)
    52→  } finally {
    53→    releaseLock()
    54→  }
    55→}
    56→
    57→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    58→// Heartbeat orchestration
    59→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    60→
    61→export async function runHeartbeat(config: Config): Promise<number> {
    62→  const logger = getLogger()
    63→
    64→  if (config.projects.length === 0) {
    65→    logger.info('No projects registered in config.toml. Nothing to do.')
    66→    return 0
    67→  }
    68→
    69→  logger.info(`Heartbeat started. ${config.projects.length} project(s) registered.`)
    70→
    71→  for (const entry of config.projects) {
    72→    const projectPath = resolve(entry.path)
    73→    if (!existsSync(projectPath)) {
    74→      logger.warn(`Project path does not exist, skipping: ${projectPath}`)
    75→      continue
    76→    }
    77→    try {
    78→      await processProject(config, projectPath, entry.name || (projectPath.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''))
    79→    } catch (err: unknown) {
    80→      logger.exception(`Error processing project: ${projectPath}`, err)
    81→      writeAlertWithThreshold(
    82→        toPosixPath(projectPath),
    83→        'push_failed',
    84→        `Heartbeat error for project: ${projectPath.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''}`,
    85→      )
    86→    }
    87→  }
    88→
    89→  logger.info('Heartbeat finished.')
    90→  return 0
    91→}
    92→
    93→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    94→// Per-project processing
    95→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    96→
    97→export async function processProject(config: Config, projectPath: string, projectName: string): Promise<void> {
    98→  const logger = getLogger()
    99→  const repoSlug = slugify(projectName, 'project')
   100→  const globalRoot = defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
   101→
   102→  const discovered = discoverSourceFiles()
   103→  let importedCount = 0
   104→
   105→  for (const [client, source] of discovered) {
   106→    let parsed: ParsedTranscript
   107→    try {
   108→      parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
   109→    } catch {
   110→      logger.debug(`Failed to parse ${source}, skipping.`)
   111→      continue
   112→    }
   113→
   114→    if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) continue
   115→    if (!transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, projectPath, repoSlug)) continue
   116→
   117→    scanSensitive(parsed, projectPath)
   118→
   119→    try {
   120→      await importTranscript(parsed, projectPath, globalRoot, repoSlug, 'not-set', true)
   121→      importedCount++
   122→    } catch {
   123→      logger.exception(`Failed to import transcript: ${source}`)
   124→    }
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  if (importedCount === 0) {
   128→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No new transcripts to import.`)
   129→    return
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Imported ${importedCount} transcript(s).`)
   133→  gitCommitAndPush(config, projectPath, projectName, importedCount)
   134→}
   135→
   136→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   137→// Sensitive pattern scanning
   138→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   139→
   140→export function scanSensitive(parsed: ParsedTranscript, projectPath: string): void {
   141→  const logger = getLogger()
   142→  for (const msg of parsed.messages) {
   143→    for (const pattern of SENSITIVE_PATTERNS) {
   144→      if (pattern.test(msg.text)) {
   145→        logger.warn(
   146→          `Sensitive pattern detected in transcript ${parsed.source_path} (project: ${projectPath.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''}, role: ${msg.role})`,
   147→        )
   148→        writeAlert(
   149→          toPosixPath(projectPath),
   150→          'sensitive_match',
   151→          `Sensitive pattern in transcript: ${parsed.source_path.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''}`,
   152→        )
   153→        return
   154→      }
   155→    }
   156→  }
   157→}
   158→
   159→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   160→// Git operations
   161→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   162→
   163→export function gitCommitAndPush(config: Config, projectPath: string, projectName: string, count: number): void {
   164→  const logger = getLogger()
   165→
   166→  const status = git(projectPath, 'status', '--porcelain', 'Memory/')
   167→  if (!status.trim()) {
   168→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No git changes in Memory/.`)
   169→    return
   170→  }
   171→
   172→  git(projectPath, 'add', 'Memory/')
   173→  git(projectPath, 'commit', '-m', `memorytree(transcripts): import ${count} transcript(s)`)
   174→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Committed ${count} transcript import(s).`)
   175→
   176→  if (!config.auto_push) {
   177→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] auto_push disabled, skipping push.`)
   178→    return
   179→  }
   180→
   181→  const remotes = git(projectPath, 'remote')
   182→  if (!remotes.trim()) {
   183→    logger.warn(`[${projectName}] No git remote configured, skipping push.`)
   184→    writeAlert(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'no_remote', 'Push skipped: no Git remote configured.')
   185→    return
   186→  }
   187→
   188→  if (!tryPush(projectPath, projectName)) {
   189→    logger.warn(`[${projectName}] Push failed, retrying once...`)
   190→    if (!tryPush(projectPath, projectName)) {
   191→      logger.error(`[${projectName}] Push failed after retry.`)
   192→      writeAlertWithThreshold(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'push_failed', 'Push failed after retry.')
   193→      return
   194→    }
   195→  }
   196→
   197→  resetFailureCount(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'push_failed')
   198→}
   199→
   200→export function tryPush(projectPath: string, projectName: string): boolean {
   201→  try {
   202→    git(projectPath, 'push')
   203→    getLogger().info(`[${projectName}] Pushed successfully.`)
   204→    return true
   205→  } catch {
   206→    return false
   207→  }
   208→}

1→/**
     2→ * PID-based lock file for heartbeat single-instance enforcement.
     3→ * Port of scripts/_lock_utils.py
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import {
     7→  closeSync,
     8→  constants,
     9→  existsSync,
    10→  mkdirSync,
    11→  openSync,
    12→  readFileSync,
    13→  unlinkSync,
    14→  writeSync,
    15→} from 'node:fs'
    16→import { homedir } from 'node:os'
    17→import { dirname, resolve } from 'node:path'
    18→import { execFileSync } from 'node:child_process'
    19→
    20→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    21→// Path helpers
    22→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    23→
    24→export function lockPath(): string {
    25→  return resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'heartbeat.lock')
    26→}
    27→
    28→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    29→// Lock acquisition
    30→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    31→
    32→/**
    33→ * Try to acquire the heartbeat lock. Returns `true` on success.
    34→ *
    35→ * If the lock file already exists, the stored PID is checked:
    36→ * - alive process  -> return false (already running)
    37→ * - dead process   -> reclaim the stale lock
    38→ * - corrupt file   -> remove and retry
    39→ *
    40→ * Uses `O_CREAT | O_EXCL` to prevent TOCTOU races.
    41→ */
    42→export function acquireLock(): boolean {
    43→  const path = lockPath()
    44→  mkdirSync(dirname(path), { recursive: true })
    45→
    46→  if (existsSync(path)) {
    47→    let storedPid: number | undefined
    48→    try {
    49→      const raw = readFileSync(path, 'utf-8').trim()
    50→      storedPid = parseInt(raw, 10)
    51→      if (!Number.isFinite(storedPid)) {
    52→        storedPid = undefined
    53→      }
    54→    } catch {
    55→      // Corrupt lock file — treat as stale
    56→      storedPid = undefined
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    if (storedPid === undefined) {
    60→      // Corrupt or unreadable lock file — remove it
    61→      removeLockFile(path)
    62→    } else {
    63→      if (isProcessAlive(storedPid)) {
    64→        return false
    65→      }
    66→      // Stale lock from a dead process — reclaim
    67→      removeLockFile(path)
    68→    }
    69→  }
    70→
    71→  // Use exclusive create to prevent TOCTOU race
    72→  try {
    73→    const fd = openSync(path, constants.O_CREAT | constants.O_EXCL | constants.O_WRONLY)
    74→    const pidBytes = Buffer.from(String(process.pid), 'utf-8')
    75→    writeSync(fd, pidBytes)
    76→    closeSync(fd)
    77→  } catch {
    78→    // Another process created the lock between our check and create,
    79→    // or an OS-level I/O error occurred.
    80→    return false
    81→  }
    82→  return true
    83→}
    84→
    85→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    86→// Lock release
    87→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    88→
    89→/** Release the heartbeat lock. */
    90→export function releaseLock(): void {
    91→  removeLockFile(lockPath())
    92→}
    93→
    94→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    95→// Lock inspection
    96→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    97→
    98→/** Read the PID from the lock file, or `null` if not locked / corrupt. */
    99→export function readLockPid(): number | null {
   100→  const path = lockPath()
   101→  if (!existsSync(path)) {
   102→    return null
   103→  }
   104→  try {
   105→    const raw = readFileSync(path, 'utf-8').trim()
   106→    const pid = parseInt(raw, 10)
   107→    return Number.isFinite(pid) ? pid : null
   108→  } catch {
   109→    return null
   110→  }
   111→}
   112→
   113→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   114→// Process liveness
   115→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   116→
   117→/** Check whether a process with the given PID is still running. */
   118→export function isProcessAlive(pid: number): boolean {
   119→  if (pid <= 0) {
   120→    return false
   121→  }
   122→  if (process.platform === 'win32') {
   123→    return isProcessAliveWindows(pid)
   124→  }
   125→  return isProcessAliveUnix(pid)
   126→}
   127→
   128→function isProcessAliveUnix(pid: number): boolean {
   129→  try {
   130→    process.kill(pid, 0)
   131→    return true
   132→  } catch (err: unknown) {
   133→    if (err instanceof Error && 'code' in err) {
   134→      // EPERM means the process exists but we lack permission to signal it
   135→      if ((err as NodeJS.ErrnoException).code === 'EPERM') {
   136→        return true
   137→      }
   138→    }
   139→    // ESRCH or any other error means the process does not exist
   140→    return false
   141→  }
   142→}
   143→
   144→function isProcessAliveWindows(pid: number): boolean {
   145→  try {
   146→    const output = execFileSync('tasklist', ['/FI', `PID eq ${pid}`, '/NH'], {
   147→      encoding: 'utf-8',
   148→      timeout: 5000,
   149→      windowsHide: true,
   150→    })
   151→    // tasklist prints "INFO: No tasks are running..." when no match is found.
   152→    // Otherwise, the output contains the PID as a number in the line.
   153→    return output.includes(String(pid))
   154→  } catch {
   155→    return false
   156→  }
   157→}
   158→
   159→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   160→// Internal helpers
   161→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   162→
   163→function removeLockFile(path: string): void {
   164→  try {
   165→    unlinkSync(path)
   166→  } catch {
   167→    // Ignore errors — file may already be gone
   168→  }
   169→}
   170→

    54→function utcTimestamp(): string {

    58→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    59→// Read / Write alerts
    60→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    62→export function readAlerts(): readonly Alert[] {
    63→  const path = alertsPath()
    64→  if (!existsSync(path)) {
    65→    return []
    66→  }
    67→  try {
    68→    const text = readFileSync(path, 'utf-8')
    69→    const data: unknown = JSON.parse(text)
    70→    if (!Array.isArray(data)) {
    71→      return []
    72→    }
    73→    return data as Alert[]
    74→  } catch {
    75→    return []
    76→  }
    77→}
    78→
    79→export function writeAlert(project: string, alertType: string, message: string): void {
    80→  const alerts = readAlerts()
    81→  const now = utcTimestamp()
    82→
    83→  let found = false
    84→  const updated: Alert[] = []
    85→
    86→  for (const alert of alerts) {
    87→    if (alert.project === project && alert.type === alertType) {
    88→      updated.push({
    89→        ...alert,
    90→        timestamp: now,
    91→        message,
    92→        count: (alert.count ?? 1) + 1,
    93→      })
    94→      found = true
    95→    } else {
    96→      updated.push({ ...alert })
    97→    }
    98→  }
    99→
   100→  if (!found) {
   101→    updated.push({ timestamp: now, project, type: alertType, message, count: 1 })
   102→  }
   103→
   104→  const trimmed = updated.length > MAX_ALERTS
   105→    ? updated.slice(updated.length - MAX_ALERTS)
   106→    : updated
   107→
   108→  saveAlerts(trimmed)
   109→}
   110→
   111→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   112→// Threshold-based writes
   113→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   114→
   115→export function writeAlertWithThreshold(
   116→  project: string,
   117→  alertType: string,
   118→  message: string,
   119→): void {
   120→  const counts = readFailureCounts()
   121→  const key = `${project}::${alertType}`
   122→  const current = ((counts[key] as number | undefined) ?? 0) + 1
   123→  const newCounts: Record<string, number> = { ...counts, [key]: current }
   124→  saveFailureCounts(newCounts)
   125→
   126→  if (current >= FAILURE_THRESHOLD) {
   127→    writeAlert(project, alertType, message)
   128→  }
   129→}
   130→
   131→export function resetFailureCount(project: string, alertType: string): void {
   132→  const counts = readFailureCounts()
   133→  const key = `${project}::${alertType}`
   134→  if (key in counts) {
   135→    const newCounts: Record<string, number> = {}
   136→    for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(counts)) {
   137→      if (k !== key) {
   138→        newCounts[k] = v
   139→      }
   140→    }
   141→    saveFailureCounts(newCounts)
   142→  }
   143→}
   144→

   150→  const path = alertsPath()
   151→  if (existsSync(path)) {
   152→    try {
   153→      unlinkSync(path)
   154→    } catch {
   155→      // Silently ignore removal errors (matches Python behaviour)
   156→    }
   157→  }
   158→}

   160→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   161→// Display

   164→export function formatAlertsForDisplay(alerts: readonly Record<string, unknown>[]): string {
   165→  if (alerts.length === 0) {
   166→    return ''
   167→  }
   168→  const lines: string[] = []
   169→  for (const alert of alerts) {
   170→    const count = typeof alert['count'] === 'number' ? alert['count'] : 1
   171→    const countSuffix = count > 1 ? ` (x${String(count)})` : ''
   172→    const type = typeof alert['type'] === 'string' ? alert['type'] : 'unknown'
   173→    const project = typeof alert['project'] === 'string' ? alert['project'] : '?'
   174→    const message = typeof alert['message'] === 'string' ? alert['message'] : ''
   175→    lines.push(`  [${type}] ${project}: ${message}${countSuffix}`)
   176→  }
   177→  return lines.join('\n')
   178→}
   179→
   180→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   181→// Internal — alerts persistence
   182→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

   185→  const path = alertsPath()
   186→  mkdirSync(dirname(path), { recursive: true })
   187→  writeFileSync(path, JSON.stringify(alerts, null, 2) + '\n', 'utf-8')
   188→}

   195→  const path = failureStatePath()

   197→    return {}
   198→  }
   199→  try {
   200→    const text = readFileSync(path, 'utf-8')
   201→    const data: unknown = JSON.parse(text)
   202→    if (data === null || typeof data !== 'object' || Array.isArray(data)) {
   203→      return {}
   204→    }
   205→    return data as Record<string, number>
   206→  } catch {
   207→    return {}
   208→  }
   209→}
   210→

   213→  mkdirSync(dirname(path), { recursive: true })

   215→}

1→/**
     2→ * Logging setup for heartbeat — file output + stderr.
     3→ * Port of scripts/_log_utils.py
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { appendFileSync, mkdirSync } from 'node:fs'
     7→import { homedir } from 'node:os'
     8→import { resolve } from 'node:path'
     9→
    10→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    11→// Types
    12→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    13→
    14→export type LogLevel = 'debug' | 'info' | 'warn' | 'error'
    15→
    16→export interface Logger {
    17→  debug(msg: string): void
    18→  info(msg: string): void
    19→  warn(msg: string): void
    20→  error(msg: string): void
    21→  exception(msg: string, err?: unknown): void
    22→}
    23→
    24→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    25→// Constants
    26→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    27→
    28→const LEVEL_PRIORITY: Readonly<Record<LogLevel, number>> = {
    29→  debug: 0,
    30→  info: 1,
    31→  warn: 2,
    32→  error: 3,
    33→}
    34→
    35→const LEVEL_LABELS: Readonly<Record<LogLevel, string>> = {
    36→  debug: 'DEBUG',
    37→  info: 'INFO',
    38→  warn: 'WARN',
    39→  error: 'ERROR',
    40→}
    41→
    42→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    43→// Singleton
    44→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    45→
    46→let singleton: MemoryTreeLogger | undefined
    47→
    48→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    49→// MemoryTreeLogger
    50→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    51→
    52→class MemoryTreeLogger implements Logger {
    53→  private readonly levelPriority: number
    54→  private readonly logFilePath: string | undefined
    55→
    56→  constructor(logLevel: LogLevel) {
    57→    this.levelPriority = LEVEL_PRIORITY[logLevel]
    58→
    59→    const filePath = logFilePathForToday()
    60→    const logDir = resolve(filePath, '..')
    61→    try {
    62→      mkdirSync(logDir, { recursive: true })
    63→      // Verify we can write by doing nothing — the first real append will
    64→      // confirm access.  We store the path only after the dir exists.
    65→      this.logFilePath = filePath
    66→    } catch {
    67→      // Cannot create log directory — stderr-only mode.
    68→      this.writeStderr('WARN', `Could not open log file: ${filePath}`)
    69→      this.logFilePath = undefined
    70→    }
    71→  }
    72→
    73→  debug(msg: string): void {
    74→    this.log('debug', msg)
    75→  }
    76→
    77→  info(msg: string): void {
    78→    this.log('info', msg)
    79→  }
    80→
    81→  warn(msg: string): void {
    82→    this.log('warn', msg)
    83→  }
    84→
    85→  error(msg: string): void {
    86→    this.log('error', msg)
    87→  }
    88→
    89→  exception(msg: string, err?: unknown): void {
    90→    if (err instanceof Error && err.stack) {
    91→      this.log('error', `${msg}\n${err.stack}`)
    92→    } else if (err !== undefined) {
    93→      this.log('error', `${msg}\n${String(err)}`)
    94→    } else {
    95→      this.log('error', msg)
    96→    }
    97→  }
    98→
    99→  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   100→  // Internal
   101→  // -----------------------------------------------------------------------
   102→
   103→  private log(level: LogLevel, msg: string): void {
   104→    if (LEVEL_PRIORITY[level] < this.levelPriority) {
   105→      return
   106→    }
   107→
   108→    const label = LEVEL_LABELS[level]
   109→    const formatted = `${timestamp()} [${label}] ${msg}`
   110→
   111→    this.writeStderr(label, msg)
   112→    this.writeFile(formatted)
   113→  }
   114→
   115→  private writeStderr(_label: string, _msg: string): void {
   116→    // Use the pre-formatted line for consistency.  We rebuild here so the
   117→    // standalone warning in the constructor can also call this without a
   118→    // full formatted line.
   119→    const line = `${timestamp()} [${_label}] ${_msg}\n`
   120→    process.stderr.write(line)
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  private writeFile(formatted: string): void {
   124→    if (this.logFilePath === undefined) {
   125→      return
   126→    }
   127→    try {
   128→      appendFileSync(this.logFilePath, formatted + '\n', 'utf-8')
   129→    } catch {
   130→      // Silently ignore file-write errors — stderr is the primary channel.
   131→    }
   132→  }
   133→}
   134→
   135→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   136→// Public API
   137→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   138→
   139→/**
   140→ * Create (or return existing) singleton logger.
   141→ *
   142→ * The `logLevel` parameter is only used on the *first* call.  Subsequent
   143→ * calls return the existing logger regardless of the level argument.
   144→ */
   145→export function setupLogging(logLevel: LogLevel = 'info'): Logger {
   146→  if (singleton !== undefined) {
   147→    return singleton
   148→  }
   149→  singleton = new MemoryTreeLogger(resolveLevel(logLevel))
   150→  return singleton
   151→}
   152→
   153→/**
   154→ * Return the singleton logger.  If `setupLogging` has not been called yet
   155→ * the logger is auto-created with default settings (`info` level).
   156→ */
   157→export function getLogger(): Logger {
   158→  if (singleton === undefined) {
   159→    singleton = new MemoryTreeLogger(resolveLevel('info'))
   160→  }
   161→  return singleton
   162→}
   163→
   164→/**
   165→ * Reset the singleton — primarily useful for tests.
   166→ */
   167→export function _resetLogger(): void {
   168→  singleton = undefined
   169→}
   170→
   171→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   172→// Internal helpers
   173→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   174→
   175→function resolveLevel(level: string): LogLevel {
   176→  const lower = level.toLowerCase()
   177→  const mapping: Record<string, LogLevel> = {
   178→    debug: 'debug',
   179→    info: 'info',
   180→    warn: 'warn',
   181→    warning: 'warn',
   182→    error: 'error',
   183→  }
   184→  return mapping[lower] ?? 'info'
   185→}
   186→
   187→function logFilePathForToday(): string {
   188→  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10) // YYYY-MM-DD in UTC
   189→  return resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'logs', `heartbeat-${today}.log`)
   190→}
   191→
   192→function timestamp(): string {
   193→  // Produce YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS in UTC matching the Python datefmt.
   194→  const now = new Date()
   195→  const y = now.getUTCFullYear()
   196→  const mo = String(now.getUTCMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
   197→  const d = String(now.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0')
   198→  const h = String(now.getUTCHours()).padStart(2, '0')
   199→  const mi = String(now.getUTCMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')
   200→  const s = String(now.getUTCSeconds()).padStart(2, '0')
   201→  return `${y}-${mo}-${d}T${h}:${mi}:${s}`
   202→}

    66→    return defaultConfig()
    67→  }
    68→  return parseRaw(raw)
    69→}
    70→
    71→export function saveConfig(cfg: Config): void {
    72→  const path = configPath()
    73→  mkdirSync(dirname(path), { recursive: true })
    74→
    75→  const lines: string[] = [
    76→    `heartbeat_interval = "${cfg.heartbeat_interval}"`,
    77→    `auto_push = ${cfg.auto_push ? 'true' : 'false'}`,
    78→    `log_level = "${cfg.log_level}"`,
    79→  ]
    80→
    81→  if (cfg.watch_dirs.length > 0) {
    82→    const items = cfg.watch_dirs.map(d => `"${d}"`).join(', ')
    83→    lines.push(`watch_dirs = [${items}]`)
    84→  } else {
    85→    lines.push('watch_dirs = []')
    86→  }
    87→
    88→  lines.push('')
    89→  for (const project of cfg.projects) {
    90→    lines.push('[[projects]]')
    91→    lines.push(`path = "${project.path}"`)
    92→    if (project.name) {
    93→      lines.push(`name = "${project.name}"`)
    94→    }
    95→    lines.push('')
    96→  }
    97→
    98→  writeFileSync(path, lines.join('\n') + '\n', 'utf-8')
    99→}
   100→
   101→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   102→// Interval parsing
   103→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   104→
   105→export function intervalToSeconds(interval: string): number {
   106→  const match = interval.trim().toLowerCase().match(/^(\d+)\s*(s|m|h)$/)
   107→  if (!match) {
   108→    return intervalToSeconds(DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
   109→  }
   110→  const value = parseInt(match[1]!, 10)
   111→  const unit = match[2]!
   112→  if (value <= 0) {
   113→    return intervalToSeconds(DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
   114→  }
   115→  const multiplier: Record<string, number> = { s: 1, m: 60, h: 3600 }
   116→  return value * (multiplier[unit] ?? 60)
   117→}
   118→
   119→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   120→// Project registration
   121→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   122→
   123→export function registerProject(cfg: Config, repoPath: string): Config {
   124→  const resolved = toPosixPath(resolve(repoPath))
   125→  for (const entry of cfg.projects) {
   126→    if (toPosixPath(resolve(entry.path)) === resolved) {
   127→      return cfg
   128→    }
   129→  }
   130→  const name = resolved.split('/').pop() ?? ''
   131→  return {
   132→    ...cfg,
   133→    projects: [...cfg.projects, { path: resolved, name }],
   134→  }
   135→}
   136→
   137→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   138→// Internal helpers
   139→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   140→
   141→function defaultConfig(): Config {
   142→  return {
   143→    heartbeat_interval: DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL,
   144→    watch_dirs: [],
   145→    projects: [],
   146→    auto_push: DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH,
   147→    log_level: DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL,
   148→  }
   149→}
   150→
   151→function parseRaw(raw: Record<string, unknown>): Config {
   152→  let interval = raw['heartbeat_interval']
   153→  if (typeof interval !== 'string' || !isValidInterval(interval)) {
   154→    interval = DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL
   155→  }
   156→
   157→  let autoPush = raw['auto_push']
   158→  if (typeof autoPush !== 'boolean') {
   159→    autoPush = DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH
   160→  }
   161→
   162→  let logLevel = raw['log_level']
   163→  if (typeof logLevel !== 'string' || !VALID_LOG_LEVELS.has(logLevel.toLowerCase())) {
   164→    logLevel = DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL
   165→  }
   166→  logLevel = (logLevel as string).toLowerCase()
   167→
   168→  const watchDirs: string[] = []
   169→  const rawDirs = raw['watch_dirs']
   170→  if (Array.isArray(rawDirs)) {
   171→    for (const d of rawDirs) {
   172→      if (typeof d === 'string') watchDirs.push(d)
   173→    }
   174→  }
   175→
   176→  const projects: ProjectEntry[] = []
   177→  const rawProjects = raw['projects']
   178→  if (Array.isArray(rawProjects)) {
   179→    for (const entry of rawProjects) {
   180→      if (entry !== null && typeof entry === 'object' && !Array.isArray(entry)) {
   181→        const rec = entry as Record<string, unknown>
   182→        if (typeof rec['path'] === 'string') {
   183→          projects.push({
   184→            path: rec['path'] as string,
   185→            name: String(rec['name'] ?? ''),
   186→          })
   187→        }
   188→      }
   189→    }
   190→  }
   191→
   192→  return {
   193→    heartbeat_interval: interval as string,
   194→    watch_dirs: watchDirs,
   195→    projects,
   196→    auto_push: autoPush as boolean,
   197→    log_level: logLevel as string,
   198→  }
   199→}
   200→
   201→function isValidInterval(value: string): boolean {
   202→  const match = value.trim().toLowerCase().match(/^(\d+)\s*(s|m|h)$/)
   203→  if (!match) return false
   204→  return parseInt(match[1]!, 10) > 0
   205→}

1→/**
     2→ * Subprocess execution wrapper for git and other commands.
     3→ * Port of heartbeat.py _git() and daemon subprocess calls.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { execFileSync } from 'node:child_process'
     7→
     8→export interface ExecResult {
     9→  stdout: string
    10→  exitCode: number
    11→}
    12→
    13→export function execCommand(
    14→  command: string,
    15→  args: readonly string[],
    16→  options?: { cwd?: string; timeout?: number; allowFailure?: boolean },
    17→): string {
    18→  const cwd = options?.cwd
    19→  const timeout = options?.timeout ?? 120_000
    20→  const allowFailure = options?.allowFailure ?? false
    21→
    22→  try {
    23→    const stdout = execFileSync(command, [...args], {
    24→      cwd,
    25→      timeout,
    26→      encoding: 'utf-8',
    27→      stdio: ['pipe', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
    28→    })
    29→    return stdout
    30→  } catch (err: unknown) {
    31→    if (allowFailure) {
    32→      const e = err as { stdout?: string }
    33→      return typeof e.stdout === 'string' ? e.stdout : ''
    34→    }
    35→    throw err
    36→  }
    37→}
    38→
    39→export function git(cwd: string, ...args: string[]): string {
    40→  const allowFailure = args[0] === 'status' || args[0] === 'remote'
    41→  return execCommand('git', args, { cwd, allowFailure })
    42→}

    21→export async function importTranscript(
    22→  parsed: ParsedTranscript,
    23→  root: string,
    24→  globalRoot: string,
    25→  projectSlug: string,
    26→  rawUploadPermission: string,
    27→  mirrorToRepo = true,
    28→): Promise<ManifestEntry> {
    29→  const importedAt = normalizeTimestamp(new Date())
    30→  const rawSha256 = sha256File(parsed.source_path)
    31→  const sessionLabel = slugify(
    32→    parsed.session_id,
    33→    slugify(stemOf(parsed.source_path), 'session'),
    34→  )
    35→  const artifactStem = `${sessionLabel}__${rawSha256.slice(0, 8)}`
    36→  const sourceSuffix = extname(parsed.source_path) || '.txt'
    37→
    38→  const [yearToken, monthToken] = timestampPartition(parsed.started_at || importedAt)
    39→
    40→  const repoRoot = join(root, 'Memory', '06_transcripts')
    41→  const repoRawPath = join(repoRoot, 'raw', parsed.client, yearToken, monthToken, `${artifactStem}${sourceSuffix}`)
    42→  const repoCleanPath = join(repoRoot, 'clean', parsed.client, yearToken, monthToken, `${artifactStem}.md`)
    43→  const repoManifestPath = join(repoRoot, 'manifests', parsed.client, yearToken, monthToken, `${artifactStem}.json`)
    44→
    45→  const globalRawPath = join(globalRoot, 'raw', parsed.client, projectSlug, yearToken, monthToken, `${artifactStem}${sourceSuffix}`)
    46→  const globalCleanPath = join(globalRoot, 'clean', parsed.client, projectSlug, yearToken, monthToken, `${artifactStem}.md`)
    47→  const globalManifestPath = join(globalRoot, 'index', 'manifests', parsed.client, projectSlug, yearToken, monthToken, `${artifactStem}.json`)
    48→  const globalEventLogPath = join(globalRoot, 'index', 'sessions.jsonl')
    49→  const globalDbPath = join(globalRoot, 'index', 'search.sqlite')
    50→
    51→  for (const p of [globalRawPath, globalCleanPath, globalManifestPath, globalEventLogPath, globalDbPath]) {
    52→    mkdirSync(dirname(p), { recursive: true })
    53→  }
    54→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
    55→    for (const p of [repoRawPath, repoCleanPath, repoManifestPath]) {
    56→      mkdirSync(dirname(p), { recursive: true })
    57→    }
    58→  }
    59→
    60→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
    61→    copyFile(parsed.source_path, repoRawPath)
    62→  }
    63→  copyFile(parsed.source_path, globalRawPath)
    64→
    65→  let manifest: ManifestEntry = {
    66→    client: parsed.client,
    67→    project: projectSlug,
    68→    session_id: parsed.session_id,
    69→    title: parsed.title,
    70→    started_at: parsed.started_at,
    71→    imported_at: importedAt,
    72→    cwd: parsed.cwd,
    73→    branch: parsed.branch,
    74→    raw_source_path: toPosixPath(parsed.source_path),
    75→    raw_sha256: rawSha256,
    76→    raw_upload_permission: rawUploadPermission,
    77→    repo_raw_path: mirrorToRepo ? toPosixPath(relative(root, repoRawPath)) : '',
    78→    repo_clean_path: mirrorToRepo ? toPosixPath(relative(root, repoCleanPath)) : '',
    79→    repo_manifest_path: mirrorToRepo ? toPosixPath(relative(root, repoManifestPath)) : '',
    80→    global_raw_path: toPosixPath(globalRawPath),
    81→    global_clean_path: toPosixPath(globalCleanPath),
    82→    global_manifest_path: toPosixPath(globalManifestPath),
    83→    message_count: parsed.messages.length,
    84→    tool_event_count: parsed.tool_events.length,
    85→    cleaning_mode: 'deterministic-code',
    86→    repo_mirror_enabled: mirrorToRepo,
    87→  }
    88→
    89→  const existingGlobalManifest = loadJson(globalManifestPath)
    90→  manifest = preserveExistingImportTimestamp(existingGlobalManifest, manifest)
    91→
    92→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
    93→    writeCleanMarkdown(parsed, manifest, repoCleanPath)
    94→  }
    95→  writeCleanMarkdown(parsed, manifest, globalCleanPath)
    96→  const manifestRecord = { ...manifest } as Record<string, unknown>
    97→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
    98→    writeJson(repoManifestPath, manifestRecord)
    99→  }
   100→  const appendToEventLog = existingGlobalManifest === null || !deepEqual(existingGlobalManifest, manifestRecord)
   101→  writeJson(globalManifestPath, manifestRecord)
   102→  if (appendToEventLog) {
   103→    appendJsonl(globalEventLogPath, manifestRecord)
   104→  }
   105→  await upsertSearchIndex(globalDbPath, manifest)
   106→
   107→  return manifest
   108→}

   110→export function transcriptHasContent(parsed: ParsedTranscript): boolean {
   111→  return parsed.messages.length > 0 || parsed.tool_events.length > 0
   112→}
   113→
   114→export function writeCleanMarkdown(parsed: ParsedTranscript, manifest: ManifestEntry, filePath: string): void {
   115→  const lines: string[] = [
   116→    '---',
   117→    `client: ${manifest.client}`,
   118→    `project: ${manifest.project}`,
   119→    `session_id: ${manifest.session_id}`,
   120→    `title: ${yamlEscape(manifest.title)}`,
   121→    `started_at: ${manifest.started_at}`,
   122→    `imported_at: ${manifest.imported_at}`,
   123→    `cwd: ${yamlEscape(manifest.cwd)}`,
   124→    `branch: ${yamlEscape(manifest.branch)}`,
   125→    `raw_source_path: ${yamlEscape(manifest.raw_source_path)}`,
   126→    `raw_sha256: ${manifest.raw_sha256}`,
   127→    `raw_upload_permission: ${manifest.raw_upload_permission}`,
   128→    `cleaning_mode: ${manifest.cleaning_mode}`,
   129→    '---',
   130→    '',
   131→    `# ${manifest.title || manifest.session_id}`,
   132→    '',
   133→    '## Metadata',
   134→    `- Client: \`${manifest.client}\``,
   135→    `- Project: \`${manifest.project}\``,
   136→    `- Session ID: \`${manifest.session_id}\``,
   137→    `- Started At: \`${manifest.started_at}\``,
   138→    `- Imported At: \`${manifest.imported_at}\``,
   139→    `- Raw SHA256: \`${manifest.raw_sha256}\``,
   140→    `- Raw Source: \`${manifest.raw_source_path}\``,
   141→    `- Repo Raw Path: \`${manifest.repo_raw_path}\``,
   142→    `- Repo Clean Path: \`${manifest.repo_clean_path}\``,
   143→    '',
   144→    '## Messages',
   145→  ]
   146→
   147→  if (parsed.messages.length > 0) {
   148→    for (let i = 0; i < parsed.messages.length; i++) {
   149→      const message = parsed.messages[i]!
   150→      lines.push(
   151→        `### ${i + 1}. ${message.role}`,
   152→        `- Timestamp: \`${message.timestamp ?? manifest.started_at}\``,
   153→        '',
   154→        message.text,
   155→        '',
   156→      )
   157→    }
   158→  } else {
   159→    lines.push(
   160→      'No user or assistant messages were extracted deterministically from the source transcript.',
   161→      '',
   162→    )
   163→  }
   164→
   165→  lines.push('## Tool Events')
   166→  if (parsed.tool_events.length > 0) {
   167→    for (const event of parsed.tool_events) {
   168→      lines.push(`- \`${event.timestamp ?? manifest.started_at}\` ${event.summary}`)
   169→    }
   170→  } else {
   171→    lines.push('- No tool events were extracted.')
   172→  }
   173→  lines.push('')
   174→
   175→  writeFileSync(filePath, lines.join('\n'), 'utf-8')
   176→}
   177→
   178→export function preserveExistingImportTimestamp(
   179→  existing: Record<string, unknown> | null,
   180→  payload: ManifestEntry,
   181→): ManifestEntry {
   182→  if (existing === null) return payload
   183→  const payloadRecord = { ...payload } as Record<string, unknown>
   184→  if (!deepEqual(manifestSignature(existing), manifestSignature(payloadRecord))) return payload
   185→  const importedAt = existing['imported_at']
   186→  if (typeof importedAt === 'string' && importedAt) {
   187→    return { ...payload, imported_at: importedAt }
   188→  }
   189→  return payload
   190→}
   191→
   192→export function manifestSignature(payload: Record<string, unknown>): Record<string, unknown> {
   193→  const result: Record<string, unknown> = {}
   194→  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(payload)) {
   195→    if (key !== 'imported_at') {
   196→      result[key] = value
   197→    }
   198→  }
   199→  return result
   200→}
   201→
   202→export function manifestChanged(filePath: string, payload: Record<string, unknown>): boolean {
   203→  if (!existsSync(filePath)) return true
   204→  try {
   205→    const current = JSON.parse(readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')) as Record<string, unknown>
   206→    return !deepEqual(current, payload)
   207→  } catch {
   208→    return true
   209→  }
   210→}
   211→
   212→export function writeJson(filePath: string, payload: Record<string, unknown>): void {
   213→  writeFileSync(filePath, JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2) + '\n', 'utf-8')
   214→}
   215→
   216→export function appendJsonl(filePath: string, payload: Record<string, unknown>): void {
   217→  appendFileSync(filePath, JSON.stringify(payload) + '\n', 'utf-8')
   218→}
   219→
   220→export function copyFile(source: string, destination: string): void {
   221→  if (source === destination) return
   222→  copyFileSync(source, destination)
   223→}
   224→
   225→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   226→// Internal helpers
   227→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   228→
   229→function stemOf(filePath: string): string {
   230→  const base = filePath.replace(/\\/g, '/').split('/').pop() ?? ''
   231→  const ext = extname(base)
   232→  return ext ? base.slice(0, -ext.length) : base
   233→}
   234→
   235→function deepEqual(a: unknown, b: unknown): boolean {
   236→  if (a === b) return true
   237→  if (a === null || b === null || typeof a !== typeof b) return false
   238→  if (typeof a !== 'object') return false
   239→  if (Array.isArray(a) !== Array.isArray(b)) return false
   240→  const aObj = a as Record<string, unknown>
   241→  const bObj = b as Record<string, unknown>
   242→  const aKeys = Object.keys(aObj)
   243→  const bKeys = Object.keys(bObj)
   244→  if (aKeys.length !== bKeys.length) return false
   245→  return aKeys.every(key => deepEqual(aObj[key], bObj[key]))
   246→}

     4→ */

     6→import { readFileSync, statSync } from 'node:fs'
     7→import { basename, extname } from 'node:path'
     8→
     9→import type { Client, ParsedTranscript, TranscriptMessage, TranscriptToolEvent } from '../types/transcript.js'
    10→import { toPosixPath } from '../utils/path.js'
    11→import {
    12→  SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES,
    13→  TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES,
    14→  TOOL_RESULT_TYPES,
    15→  TOOL_USE_TYPES,
    16→  deduplicateMessages,
    17→  deduplicateToolEvents,
    18→  earliestTimestamp,
    19→  ensureDict,
    20→  ensureList,
    21→  extractGeminiText,
    22→  extractTextBlocks,
    23→  findFirstMappingWithKeys,
    24→  getNested,
    25→  joinParagraphs,
    26→  loadJsonl,
    27→  normalizeTimestamp,
    28→  summarizeValue,
    29→} from './common.js'
    30→
    31→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    32→// Client inference + dispatch
    33→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    34→
    35→export function inferClient(client: string, sourcePath: string): Client {
    36→  if (client !== 'auto') {
    37→    return client as Client
    38→  }
    39→  const normalized = toPosixPath(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    40→  const fileName = basename(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    41→  if (normalized.includes('/.codex/') || fileName.startsWith('rollout-')) {
    42→    return 'codex'
    43→  }
    44→  if (normalized.includes('/.claude/') || normalized.includes('/projects/')) {
    45→    return 'claude'
    46→  }
    47→  if (normalized.includes('/.gemini/') || normalized.includes('checkpoint')) {
    48→    return 'gemini'
    49→  }
    50→  throw new Error(`could not infer transcript client from source path: ${sourcePath}`)
    51→}
    52→
    53→export function parseTranscript(client: string, sourcePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    54→  const resolved = inferClient(client, sourcePath)
    55→  if (resolved === 'codex') {
    56→    return parseCodexTranscript(sourcePath)
    57→  }
    58→  if (resolved === 'claude') {
    59→    return parseClaudeTranscript(sourcePath)
    60→  }
    61→  if (resolved === 'gemini') {
    62→    return parseGeminiTranscript(sourcePath)
    63→  }
    64→  throw new Error(`unsupported transcript client: ${resolved}`)
    65→}
    66→
    67→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    68→// Codex parser
    69→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    71→export function parseCodexTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
    72→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
    73→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
    74→  let sessionId = stem
    75→  let title = stem
    76→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
    77→  let cwd = ''
    78→  let branch = ''
    79→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
    80→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
    81→
    82→  for (const record of records) {
    83→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
    84→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
    85→
    86→    if (recordType === 'session_meta') {
    87→      const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
    88→      sessionId = String(payload['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
    89→      title = String(payload['thread_name'] ?? '') || String(payload['title'] ?? '') || title
    90→      startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, payload['timestamp'])
    91→      cwd = String(payload['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
    92→      branch = String(getNested(payload, 'git', 'branch') ?? '') || branch
    93→      continue
    94→    }
    95→
    96→    if (recordType !== 'response_item' && recordType !== 'event_msg') {
    97→      continue
    98→    }
    99→
   100→    const payload = ensureDict(record['payload'])
   101→    const payloadType = String(payload['type'] ?? '')
   102→
   103→    if (payloadType === 'message') {
   104→      const role = String(payload['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   105→      if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') {
   106→        const text = extractTextBlocks(payload['content'])
   107→        if (text) {
   108→          messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   109→        }
   110→      }
   111→      continue
   112→    }
   113→
   114→    if (payloadType === 'user_message' || payloadType === 'agent_message') {
   115→      const role = payloadType === 'user_message' ? 'user' : 'assistant'
   116→      const text = String(payload['message'] ?? '').trim()
   117→      if (text) {
   118→        messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   119→      }
   120→      continue
   121→    }
   122→
   123→    if (payloadType === 'function_call') {
   124→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || 'function_call'
   125→      const args = payload['arguments'] ?? payload['input']
   126→      toolEvents.push({
   127→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(args)}`,
   128→        timestamp,
   129→      })
   130→      continue
   131→    }
   132→
   133→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call') {
   134→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call'
   135→      toolEvents.push({
   136→        summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(payload['input'])}`,
   137→        timestamp,
   138→      })
   139→      continue
   140→    }
   141→
   142→    if (payloadType === 'function_call_output') {
   143→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'function_call_output'
   144→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   145→      toolEvents.push({
   146→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   147→        timestamp,
   148→      })
   149→      continue
   150→    }
   151→
   152→    if (payloadType === 'custom_tool_call_output') {
   153→      const name = String(payload['name'] ?? '') || String(payload['call_id'] ?? '') || 'custom_tool_call_output'
   154→      const output = payload['output'] ?? payload['content']
   155→      toolEvents.push({
   156→        summary: `${name} output=${summarizeValue(output)}`,
   157→        timestamp,
   158→      })
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→
   162→  return {
   163→    client: 'codex',
   164→    session_id: sessionId,
   165→    title,
   166→    started_at: startedAt,
   167→    cwd,
   168→    branch,
   169→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   170→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   171→    source_path: filePath,
   172→  }
   173→}

   179→export function parseClaudeTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   180→  const records = loadJsonl(filePath)
   181→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   182→  let sessionId = stem
   183→  const title = stem
   184→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   185→  let cwd = ''
   186→  let branch = ''
   187→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   188→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   189→
   190→  for (const record of records) {
   191→    const recordType = String(record['type'] ?? '')
   192→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(record['timestamp'], startedAt)
   193→    sessionId = String(record['sessionId'] ?? '') || sessionId
   194→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, record['timestamp'])
   195→    cwd = String(record['cwd'] ?? '') || cwd
   196→    branch = String(record['gitBranch'] ?? '') || branch
   197→
   198→    if (recordType !== 'user' && recordType !== 'assistant') {
   199→      continue
   200→    }
   201→
   202→    const message = ensureDict(record['message'])
   203→    const role = String(message['role'] ?? '').toLowerCase() || recordType
   204→    const textParts: string[] = []
   205→    const content = message['content']
   206→
   207→    if (typeof content === 'string') {
   208→      const text = content.trim()
   209→      if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
   210→        messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   211→      }
   212→      continue
   213→    }
   214→
   215→    for (const block of ensureList(content)) {
   216→      if (typeof block === 'string') {
   217→        if (block.trim()) {
   218→          textParts.push(block.trim())
   219→        }
   220→        continue
   221→      }
   222→      if (block === null || typeof block !== 'object' || Array.isArray(block)) {
   223→        continue
   224→      }
   225→      const rec = block as Record<string, unknown>
   226→      const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   227→
   228→      if (TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   229→        const text = String(rec['text'] ?? '').trim()
   230→        if (text) {
   231→          textParts.push(text)
   232→        }
   233→        continue
   234→      }
   235→      if (SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   236→        continue
   237→      }
   238→      if (TOOL_USE_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   239→        const name = String(rec['name'] ?? '') || 'tool_use'
   240→        toolEvents.push({
   241→          summary: `${name} input=${summarizeValue(rec['input'])}`,
   242→          timestamp,
   243→        })
   244→        continue
   245→      }
   246→      if (TOOL_RESULT_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   247→        const toolUseId = String(rec['tool_use_id'] ?? '') || 'tool_result'
   248→        toolEvents.push({
   249→          summary: `${toolUseId} output=${summarizeValue(rec['content'])}`,
   250→          timestamp,
   251→        })
   252→      }
   253→    }
   254→
   255→    const text = joinParagraphs(textParts)
   256→    if ((role === 'user' || role === 'assistant') && text) {
   257→      messages.push({ role, text, timestamp })
   258→    }
   259→  }
   260→
   261→  return {
   262→    client: 'claude',
   263→    session_id: sessionId,
   264→    title,
   265→    started_at: startedAt,
   266→    cwd,
   267→    branch,
   268→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   269→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   270→    source_path: filePath,
   271→  }
   272→}

   274→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   275→// Gemini parser
   276→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   277→
   278→export function parseGeminiTranscript(filePath: string): ParsedTranscript {
   279→  const stem = basename(filePath, extname(filePath))
   280→  let sessionId = stem
   281→  const title = stem
   282→  let startedAt = normalizeTimestamp(statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000)
   283→  let cwd = ''
   284→  let branch = ''
   285→  const messages: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   286→  const toolEvents: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   287→
   288→  let payload: unknown
   289→  if (extname(filePath).toLowerCase() === '.jsonl') {
   290→    payload = loadJsonl(filePath)
   291→  } else {
   292→    payload = JSON.parse(readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')) as unknown
   293→  }
   294→
   295→  const metaKeys: ReadonlySet<string> = new Set(['sessionId', 'chatId', 'cwd', 'branch', 'timestamp'])
   296→  const firstMeta = findFirstMappingWithKeys(payload, metaKeys)
   297→  if (firstMeta !== null) {
   298→    sessionId = String(firstMeta['sessionId'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['chatId'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   299→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, firstMeta['timestamp'])
   300→    cwd = String(firstMeta['cwd'] ?? '') || String(firstMeta['projectRoot'] ?? '') || cwd
   301→    branch = String(firstMeta['branch'] ?? '') || branch
   302→  }
   303→
   304→  function visit(node: unknown): void {
   305→    if (Array.isArray(node)) {
   306→      for (const item of node) {
   307→        visit(item)
   308→      }
   309→      return
   310→    }
   311→    if (node === null || typeof node !== 'object') {
   312→      return
   313→    }
   314→    const rec = node as Record<string, unknown>
   315→
   316→    sessionId = String(rec['sessionId'] ?? '') || String(rec['chatId'] ?? '') || String(rec['id'] ?? '') || sessionId
   317→    startedAt = earliestTimestamp(startedAt, rec['timestamp'])
   318→    cwd = String(rec['cwd'] ?? '') || String(rec['projectRoot'] ?? '') || cwd
   319→    branch = String(rec['branch'] ?? '') || branch
   320→
   321→    const role = String(rec['role'] ?? rec['author'] ?? rec['sender'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   322→    const timestamp = normalizeTimestamp(rec['timestamp'], startedAt)
   323→
   324→    if (role === 'user' || role === 'assistant' || role === 'model') {
   325→      const normalizedRole = role === 'model' ? 'assistant' : role
   326→      const text = extractGeminiText(rec)
   327→      if (text) {
   328→        messages.push({ role: normalizedRole, text, timestamp })
   329→      }
   330→    }
   331→
   332→    const toolName =
   333→      getNested(rec, 'toolUse', 'name') ??
   334→      rec['toolName'] ??
   335→      rec['functionName'] ??
   336→      rec['tool']
   337→    if (toolName) {
   338→      toolEvents.push({
   339→        summary: `${String(toolName)} input=${summarizeValue(rec['args'] ?? rec['input'])}`,
   340→        timestamp,
   341→      })
   342→    }
   343→
   344→    for (const value of Object.values(rec)) {
   345→      visit(value)
   346→    }
   347→  }
   348→
   349→  visit(payload)
   350→
   351→  return {
   352→    client: 'gemini',
   353→    session_id: sessionId,
   354→    title,
   355→    started_at: startedAt,
   356→    cwd,
   357→    branch,
   358→    messages: deduplicateMessages(messages),
   359→    tool_events: deduplicateToolEvents(toolEvents),
   360→    source_path: filePath,
   361→  }
   362→}

    25→export function slugify(value: string, fallback = 'session'): string {
    26→  // eslint-disable-next-line no-control-regex
    27→  const asciiValue = value.replace(/[^\x00-\x7F]/g, '').toLowerCase()
    28→  const slug = asciiValue.replace(/[^a-z0-9._-]+/g, '-').replace(/^[-._]+|[-._]+$/g, '')
    29→  return slug || fallback
    30→}

    32→export function sha256File(filePath: string): string {
    33→  const data = readFileSync(filePath)
    34→  return createHash('sha256').update(data).digest('hex')
    35→}
    36→
    37→export function contentHash(text: string): string {
    38→  return createHash('sha256').update(text, 'utf8').digest('hex').slice(0, 16)
    39→}

    41→export function normalizeTimestamp(value: unknown, fallback?: string | null): string {
    42→  if (typeof value === 'number') {
    43→    const ms = value < 1e12 ? value * 1000 : value
    44→    const d = new Date(ms)
    45→    return formatUtcIso(d)
    46→  }
    47→
    48→  if (value instanceof Date) {
    49→    return formatUtcIso(value)
    50→  }
    51→
    52→  if (typeof value === 'string') {
    53→    const text = value.trim()
    54→    if (!text) {
    55→      return fallback ?? normalizeTimestamp(new Date())
    56→    }
    57→    const parsed = parseIsoTimestamp(text)
    58→    if (parsed !== null) {
    59→      return formatUtcIso(parsed)
    60→    }
    61→    return text
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  return fallback ?? normalizeTimestamp(new Date())
    65→}
    66→
    67→export function earliestTimestamp(current: string, candidate: unknown): string {
    68→  const normalized = normalizeTimestamp(candidate, current)
    69→  const currentDt = parseIsoTimestamp(current)
    70→  const normalizedDt = parseIsoTimestamp(normalized)
    71→  if (currentDt !== null && normalizedDt !== null) {
    72→    return normalizedDt < currentDt ? normalized : current
    73→  }
    74→  if (normalizedDt !== null) {
    75→    return normalized
    76→  }
    77→  return current || normalized
    78→}
    79→
    80→export function parseIsoTimestamp(value: string): Date | null {
    81→  if (!value) return null
    82→  const candidate = value.endsWith('Z') ? value.slice(0, -1) + '+00:00' : value
    83→  const d = new Date(candidate)
    84→  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return null
    85→  return d
    86→}
    87→
    88→export function timestampPartition(timestamp: string): [string, string] {
    89→  const d = parseIsoTimestamp(timestamp)
    90→  if (d === null) return ['unknown', 'unknown']
    91→  const year = d.getUTCFullYear().toString()
    92→  const month = (d.getUTCMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0')
    93→  return [year, month]
    94→}

    96→export function joinParagraphs(parts: Iterable<string>): string {
    97→  const cleaned: string[] = []
    98→  for (const part of parts) {
    99→    const trimmed = String(part).trim()
   100→    if (trimmed) cleaned.push(trimmed)
   101→  }
   102→  return cleaned.join('\n\n')
   103→}
   104→
   105→export function summarizeValue(value: unknown, limit = 180): string {
   106→  if (value === null || value === undefined) return 'none'
   107→  if (typeof value === 'string') {
   108→    const text = value.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim()
   109→    return truncate(text, limit)
   110→  }
   111→  let text: string
   112→  try {
   113→    text = JSON.stringify(value, Object.keys(value as Record<string, unknown>).sort())
   114→  } catch {
   115→    text = String(value)
   116→  }
   117→  text = text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim()
   118→  return truncate(text, limit)
   119→}
   120→
   121→export function truncate(text: string, limit: number): string {
   122→  return text.length <= limit ? text : text.slice(0, limit - 3) + '...'
   123→}
   124→
   125→export function yamlEscape(value: string): string {
   126→  const escaped = value.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/"/g, '\\"').replace(/\n/g, '\\n')
   127→  return `"${escaped}"`
   128→}

   134→export function ensureDict(value: unknown): Record<string, unknown> {
   135→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
   136→    return value as Record<string, unknown>
   137→  }
   138→  return {}
   139→}
   140→
   141→export function ensureList(value: unknown): unknown[] {
   142→  return Array.isArray(value) ? value : []
   143→}
   144→
   145→export function getNested(payload: Record<string, unknown>, ...keys: string[]): unknown {
   146→  let current: unknown = payload
   147→  for (const key of keys) {
   148→    if (current === null || typeof current !== 'object' || Array.isArray(current)) {
   149→      return null
   150→    }
   151→    current = (current as Record<string, unknown>)[key]
   152→  }
   153→  return current ?? null
   154→}
   155→
   156→export function loadJsonl(filePath: string): Record<string, unknown>[] {
   157→  let content: string
   158→  try {
   159→    content = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')
   160→  } catch {
   161→    return []
   162→  }
   163→  const records: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
   164→  for (const line of content.split('\n')) {
   165→    const trimmed = line.trim()
   166→    if (!trimmed) continue
   167→    try {
   168→      records.push(JSON.parse(trimmed) as Record<string, unknown>)
   169→    } catch {
   170→      continue
   171→    }
   172→  }
   173→  return records
   174→}
   175→
   176→export function loadJson(filePath: string): Record<string, unknown> | null {
   177→  if (!existsSync(filePath)) return null
   178→  try {
   179→    const text = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')
   180→    return JSON.parse(text) as Record<string, unknown>
   181→  } catch {
   182→    return null
   183→  }
   184→}
   185→
   186→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   187→// Text extraction helpers
   188→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   189→
   190→export function extractTextBlocks(blocks: unknown): string {
   191→  const parts: string[] = []
   192→  const skipTypes = new Set([...SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES, ...TOOL_USE_TYPES, ...TOOL_RESULT_TYPES])
   193→
   194→  for (const block of ensureList(blocks)) {
   195→    if (typeof block === 'string') {
   196→      const text = block.trim()
   197→      if (text) parts.push(text)
   198→      continue
   199→    }
   200→    if (block === null || typeof block !== 'object' || Array.isArray(block)) continue
   201→
   202→    const rec = block as Record<string, unknown>
   203→    const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   204→    if (skipTypes.has(blockType)) continue
   205→    if (TEXT_BLOCK_TYPES.has(blockType)) {
   206→      const text = String(rec['text'] ?? '').trim()
   207→      if (text) parts.push(text)
   208→      continue
   209→    }
   210→    const fallbackText = extractSimpleText(block)
   211→    if (fallbackText) parts.push(fallbackText)
   212→  }
   213→  return joinParagraphs(parts)
   214→}
   215→
   216→export function extractSimpleText(value: unknown): string {
   217→  if (typeof value === 'string') return value.trim()
   218→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   219→    return joinParagraphs(value.map(item => extractSimpleText(item)))
   220→  }
   221→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object') {
   222→    const rec = value as Record<string, unknown>
   223→    for (const key of ['text', 'content', 'value']) {
   224→      if (key in rec && typeof rec[key] === 'string') {
   225→        return (rec[key] as string).trim()
   226→      }
   227→    }
   228→    return ''
   229→  }
   230→  return ''
   231→}
   232→
   233→export function extractGeminiText(node: Record<string, unknown>): string {
   234→  const parts: string[] = []
   235→  for (const key of ['parts', 'content', 'text', 'message']) {
   236→    parts.push(...extractGeminiParts(node[key]))
   237→  }
   238→  return joinParagraphs(parts)
   239→}
   240→
   241→export function extractGeminiParts(value: unknown): string[] {
   242→  if (typeof value === 'string') {
   243→    const text = value.trim()
   244→    return text ? [text] : []
   245→  }
   246→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   247→    const parts: string[] = []
   248→    for (const item of value) {
   249→      parts.push(...extractGeminiParts(item))
   250→    }
   251→    return parts
   252→  }
   253→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object') {
   254→    const rec = value as Record<string, unknown>
   255→    const blockType = String(rec['type'] ?? '').toLowerCase()
   256→    const skipTypes = new Set([...SKIP_BLOCK_TYPES, ...TOOL_USE_TYPES, ...TOOL_RESULT_TYPES])
   257→    if (skipTypes.has(blockType)) return []
   258→    if ('text' in rec && typeof rec['text'] === 'string') {
   259→      const text = (rec['text'] as string).trim()
   260→      return text ? [text] : []
   261→    }
   262→    const parts: string[] = []
   263→    for (const key of ['parts', 'content']) {
   264→      if (key in rec) {
   265→        parts.push(...extractGeminiParts(rec[key]))
   266→      }
   267→    }
   268→    return parts
   269→  }
   270→  return []
   271→}
   272→
   273→export function findFirstMappingWithKeys(value: unknown, keys: ReadonlySet<string>): Record<string, unknown> | null {
   274→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
   275→    const rec = value as Record<string, unknown>
   276→    const recKeys = Object.keys(rec)
   277→    if (recKeys.some(k => keys.has(k))) return rec
   278→    for (const v of Object.values(rec)) {
   279→      const result = findFirstMappingWithKeys(v, keys)
   280→      if (result !== null) return result
   281→    }
   282→    return null
   283→  }
   284→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   285→    for (const item of value) {
   286→      const result = findFirstMappingWithKeys(item, keys)
   287→      if (result !== null) return result
   288→    }
   289→  }
   290→  return null
   291→}
   292→
   293→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   294→// Deduplication helpers
   295→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   296→
   297→export function deduplicateMessages(messages: readonly TranscriptMessage[]): TranscriptMessage[] {
   298→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   299→  const result: TranscriptMessage[] = []
   300→  for (const msg of messages) {
   301→    const sig = `${msg.timestamp ?? ''}\0${msg.role}\0${contentHash(msg.text)}`
   302→    if (!seen.has(sig)) {
   303→      seen.add(sig)
   304→      result.push(msg)
   305→    }
   306→  }
   307→  return result
   308→}
   309→
   310→export function deduplicateToolEvents(events: readonly TranscriptToolEvent[]): TranscriptToolEvent[] {
   311→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   312→  const result: TranscriptToolEvent[] = []
   313→  for (const evt of events) {
   314→    const sig = `${evt.timestamp ?? ''}\0${contentHash(evt.summary)}`
   315→    if (!seen.has(sig)) {
   316→      seen.add(sig)
   317→      result.push(evt)
   318→    }
   319→  }
   320→  return result
   321→}

   323→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   324→// Internal helpers
   325→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   326→
   327→function formatUtcIso(d: Date): string {
   328→  const year = d.getUTCFullYear()
   329→  const month = String(d.getUTCMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
   330→  const day = String(d.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0')
   331→  const hours = String(d.getUTCHours()).padStart(2, '0')
   332→  const minutes = String(d.getUTCMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')
   333→  const seconds = String(d.getUTCSeconds()).padStart(2, '0')
   334→  return `${year}-${month}-${day}T${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}Z`
   335→}

    50→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    51→// File discovery
    52→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    53→
    54→export function discoverSourceFiles(
    55→  clients?: ReadonlySet<string>,
    56→  roots?: Readonly<Record<string, string>>,
    57→): Array<[string, string]> {
    58→  const requested = clients ?? CLIENTS
    59→  const resolvedRoots = roots ?? defaultClientRoots()
    60→  const matches: Array<[string, string]> = []
    61→  const seen = new Set<string>()
    62→
    63→  for (const client of [...requested].sort()) {
    64→    const root: string | undefined = resolvedRoots[client]
    65→    if (root === undefined || !existsSync(root)) continue
    66→
    67→    const patterns = CLIENT_PATTERNS[client]
    68→    if (patterns === undefined) continue
    69→
    70→    for (const pattern of patterns) {
    71→      const paths = fg.sync(pattern, { cwd: root, absolute: true, onlyFiles: true })
    72→      for (const filePath of paths) {
    73→        const resolved = toPosixPath(resolve(filePath))
    74→        const key = resolved.toLowerCase()
    75→        if (seen.has(key)) continue
    76→        seen.add(key)
    77→        matches.push([client, resolved])
    78→      }
    79→    }
    80→  }
    81→
    82→  matches.sort((a, b) => {
    83→    const mtimeA = safeFileMtime(a[1])
    84→    const mtimeB = safeFileMtime(b[1])
    85→    if (mtimeB !== mtimeA) return mtimeB - mtimeA
    86→    const pathA = a[1].toLowerCase()
    87→    const pathB = b[1].toLowerCase()
    88→    // Reverse sort: higher path string comes first (matching Python's reverse=True)
    89→    if (pathB > pathA) return 1
    90→    if (pathB < pathA) return -1
    91→    return 0
    92→  })
    93→
    94→  return matches
    95→}

    97→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    98→// Project slug inference
    99→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   100→
   101→export function inferProjectSlug(parsed: ParsedTranscript): string {
   102→  if (parsed.cwd) {
   103→    try {
   104→      const cwdBase = basename(parsed.cwd)
   105→      return slugify(cwdBase, 'project')
   106→    } catch {
   107→      // fall through
   108→    }
   109→  }
   110→
   111→  if (parsed.client === 'claude') {
   112→    let parentName = basename(dirname(parsed.source_path)).toLowerCase()
   113→    parentName = parentName.replace(/^[a-z]--/, '')
   114→    return slugify(parentName, 'project')
   115→  }
   116→
   117→  if (parsed.client === 'gemini') {
   118→    const parentDir = basename(dirname(parsed.source_path))
   119→    if (parentDir) {
   120→      return slugify(parentDir, 'project')
   121→    }
   122→  }
   123→
   124→  return 'unknown-project'
   125→}
   126→
   127→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   128→// Repo matching
   129→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   130→
   131→export function transcriptMatchesRepo(
   132→  parsed: ParsedTranscript,
   133→  repoRoot: string,
   134→  repoSlug: string,
   135→): boolean {
   136→  const normalizedRepo = toPosixPath(resolve(repoRoot)).toLowerCase()
   137→
   138→  if (parsed.cwd) {
   139→    try {
   140→      const normalizedCwd = toPosixPath(resolve(parsed.cwd)).toLowerCase()
   141→      if (normalizedCwd === normalizedRepo) return true
   142→      // Check if repoRoot is a parent of cwd
   143→      const repoPrefix = normalizedRepo.endsWith('/')
   144→        ? normalizedRepo
   145→        : normalizedRepo + '/'
   146→      if (normalizedCwd.startsWith(repoPrefix)) return true
   147→    } catch {
   148→      // fall through
   149→    }
   150→  }
   151→
   152→  return projectSlugsMatch(inferProjectSlug(parsed), repoSlug)
   153→}
   154→
   155→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   156→// Slug matching
   157→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   158→
   159→export function projectSlugsMatch(left: string, right: string): boolean {
   160→  return Boolean(
   161→    left && right && left === right && left !== 'unknown-project',
   162→  )
   163→}
