   169→export function safeFileMtime(filePath: string): number {
   170→  try {
   171→    return statSync(filePath).mtimeMs / 1000
   172→  } catch {
   173→    return 0
   174→  }
   175→}

    77→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    81→export function buildDatetime(dateValue: string, timeValue: string): Date {
    82→  if (dateValue && timeValue) {
    83→    return new Date(`${dateValue}T${timeValue}:00`)
    84→  }
    85→  if (dateValue) {
    86→    return new Date(`${dateValue}T00:00:00`)
    87→  }
    88→  if (timeValue) {
    89→    const today = new Date()
    90→    const y = today.getFullYear()
    91→    const m = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
    92→    const d = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
    93→    return new Date(`${y}-${m}-${d}T${timeValue}:00`)
    94→  }
    95→  return new Date()
    96→}

   116→export function findExternalPolicySources(root: string): string[] {
   117→  const matches = new Set<string>()
   118→
   119→  for (const pattern of ALWAYS_POLICY_SOURCE_PATTERNS) {
   120→    const p = join(root, pattern)
   121→    if (existsSync(p) && isFile(p)) {
   122→      matches.add(toPosixPath(relative(root, p)))
   123→    }
   124→  }
   125→
   126→  for (const pattern of CONTENT_POLICY_SOURCE_PATTERNS) {
   127→    const p = join(root, pattern)
   128→    if (existsSync(p) && isFile(p) && hasPolicyContent(p)) {
   129→      matches.add(toPosixPath(relative(root, p)))
   130→    }
   131→  }
   132→
   133→  return [...matches].sort()
   134→}

   150→export function findLatestVersion(folder: string, pattern: RegExp): string | null {
   151→  if (!existsSync(folder)) return null
   152→  const versions: string[] = []
   153→  try {
   154→    for (const entry of readdirSync(folder)) {
   155→      const match = pattern.exec(entry)
   156→      if (match?.[1]) {
   157→        versions.push(match[1])
   158→      }
   159→    }
   160→  } catch {
   161→    return null
   162→  }
   163→  return versions.length > 0 ? versions.sort().pop()! : null
   164→}

   166→export function findLatestGoalFile(folder: string): string | null {
   167→  const regex = /^goal_v(\d{3})_(\d{8})\.md$/
   168→  const matches: Array<[string, string, string]> = []
   169→  if (!existsSync(folder)) return null
   170→  try {
   171→    for (const entry of readdirSync(folder)) {
   172→      const match = regex.exec(entry)
   173→      if (match) {
   174→        matches.push([match[1]!, match[2]!, join(folder, entry)])
   175→      }
   176→    }
   177→  } catch {
   178→    return null
   179→  }
   180→  if (matches.length === 0) return null
   181→  matches.sort()
   182→  return matches[matches.length - 1]![2]
   183→}

   234→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   235→// Template writing
   236→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   237→
   238→export function writeTemplate(
   239→  templatePath: string,
   240→  targetPath: string,
   241→  force: boolean,
   242→  values: Record<string, string>,
   243→): boolean {
   244→  if (existsSync(targetPath) && !force) return false
   245→  let content = readFileSync(templatePath, 'utf-8')
   246→  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(values)) {
   247→    content = content.replaceAll(`{{${key}}}`, value)
   248→  }
   249→  mkdirSync(join(targetPath, '..'), { recursive: true })
   250→  writeFileSync(targetPath, content, 'utf-8')
   251→  return true
   252→}

   254→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   255→// Scaffold paths
   256→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   257→
   258→export function resolveScaffoldPaths(root: string, dt: Date): ScaffoldPaths {
   259→  const y = dt.getFullYear()
   260→  const m = String(dt.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
   261→  const d = String(dt.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
   262→  const hh = String(dt.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')
   263→  const mm = String(dt.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')
   264→
   265→  const dateToken = `${y}${m}${d}`
   266→  const dateLabel = `${y}-${m}-${d}`
   267→  const timeLabel = `${hh}:${mm}`
   268→  const chatFilename = `${y}-${m}-${d}_${hh}-${mm}.md`
   269→
   270→  const goalDir = join(root, 'Memory', '01_goals')
   271→  const todoDir = join(root, 'Memory', '02_todos')
   272→  const chatDir = join(root, 'Memory', '03_chat_logs')
   273→
   274→  let goalVersion = findLatestVersion(goalDir, /^goal_v(\d{3})_\d{8}\.md$/)
   275→  if (goalVersion === null) goalVersion = '001'
   276→  const prevNum = parseInt(goalVersion, 10)
   277→  const previousVersion = prevNum > 1 ? `v${String(prevNum - 1).padStart(3, '0')}` : 'none'
   278→
   279→  let todoVersion = findLatestTodoVersion(todoDir, goalVersion)
   280→  if (todoVersion === null) todoVersion = '001'
   281→
   282→  const goalPath = findLatestGoalFile(goalDir) ?? join(goalDir, `goal_v${goalVersion}_${dateToken}.md`)
   283→  const todoPath = findLatestTodoFile(todoDir, goalVersion) ?? join(todoDir, `todo_v${goalVersion}_${todoVersion}_${dateToken}.md`)
   284→  const chatPath = findLatestChatLogFile(chatDir) ?? join(chatDir, chatFilename)
   285→
   286→  return {
   287→    root,
   288→    goalDir,
   289→    todoDir,
   290→    chatDir,
   291→    goalPath,
   292→    todoPath,
   293→    chatPath,

   296→    previousVersion,
   297→    dateLabel,
   298→    timeLabel,
   299→  }
   300→}
   301→
   302→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   303→// Directory creation
   304→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   305→
   306→export function createMemoryDirs(root: string): string[] {
   307→  const created: string[] = []
   308→  for (const rel of MEMORY_DIRS) {
   309→    const p = join(root, rel)
   310→    if (!existsSync(p)) {
   311→      created.push(toPosixPath(rel))
   312→    }
   313→    mkdirSync(p, { recursive: true })
   314→  }
   315→  return created
   316→}

   318→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   319→// Content scaffolding
   320→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   321→
   322→export function scaffoldContentFiles(
   323→  paths: ScaffoldPaths,
   324→  templates: string,
   325→  goalSummary: string,
   326→  projectName: string,
   327→  force: boolean,
   328→): { created: string[]; preserved: string[] } {
   329→  const created: string[] = []
   330→  const preserved: string[] = []
   331→
   332→  const pairs: Array<[string, string, Record<string, string>]> = [
   333→    [
   334→      join(templates, 'goal.md'),
   335→      paths.goalPath,
   336→      {
   337→        GOAL_VERSION: paths.goalVersion,
   338→        DATE: paths.dateLabel,
   339→        PREVIOUS_VERSION: paths.previousVersion,
   340→        GOAL_SUMMARY: goalSummary.trim(),
   341→      },
   342→    ],
   343→    [
   344→      join(templates, 'todo.md'),
   345→      paths.todoPath,
   346→      {
   347→        GOAL_VERSION: paths.goalVersion,
   348→        TODO_SUBVERSION: paths.todoVersion,
   349→        DATE: paths.dateLabel,
   350→      },
   351→    ],
   352→    [
   353→      join(templates, 'chat-log.md'),
   354→      paths.chatPath,
   355→      {
   356→        DATE: paths.dateLabel,
   357→        TIME: paths.timeLabel,
   358→        PROJECT_NAME: projectName.trim(),
   359→      },
   360→    ],
   361→  ]
   362→
   363→  for (const [templatePath, targetPath, values] of pairs) {
   364→    if (writeTemplate(templatePath, targetPath, force, values)) {
   365→      created.push(toPosixPath(relative(paths.root, targetPath)))
   366→    } else {
   367→      preserved.push(toPosixPath(relative(paths.root, targetPath)))
   368→    }
   369→  }
   370→
   371→  return { created, preserved }
   372→}

1→/**
     2→ * Locale — project language detection.
     3→ * Port of scripts/_locale_utils.py
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { existsSync, readdirSync, statSync, openSync, readSync, closeSync } from 'node:fs'
     7→import { join, extname } from 'node:path'
     8→
     9→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    10→// Constants
    11→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    12→
    13→const TEXT_EXTENSIONS: ReadonlySet<string> = new Set(['.md', '.txt'])
    14→const CJK_RE = /[\u3400-\u4dbf\u4e00-\u9fff]/g
    15→const LATIN_RE = /[A-Za-z]/g
    16→const MIN_LATIN_SIGNAL = 3
    17→
    18→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    19→// Public API
    20→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    21→
    22→export function normalizeLocale(value: string, root?: string): string {
    23→  let normalized = (value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase()
    24→  if (normalized === '' || normalized === 'auto') {
    25→    normalized = (root ? detectRepoLocale(root) : null) ?? detectSystemLocale()
    26→  }
    27→
    28→  const mapping: Record<string, string> = {
    29→    'en': 'en',
    30→    'en-us': 'en',
    31→    'en-gb': 'en',
    32→    'zh': 'zh-cn',
    33→    'zh-cn': 'zh-cn',
    34→    'zh-sg': 'zh-cn',
    35→    'zh-hans': 'zh-cn',
    36→    'zh-hant': 'zh-cn',
    37→    'zh-tw': 'zh-cn',
    38→    'zh-hk': 'zh-cn',
    39→  }
    40→  return mapping[normalized] ?? normalized
    41→}
    42→
    43→export function detectRepoLocale(root: string): string | null {
    44→  if (!existsSync(root)) return null
    45→
    46→  let zhScore = 0
    47→  let enScore = 0
    48→
    49→  for (const filePath of iterRepoTextCandidates(root)) {
    50→    const name = filePath.split(/[/\\]/).pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? ''
    51→    if (name.includes('zh-cn') || name.includes('zh_cn')) {
    52→      zhScore += 12
    53→    }
    54→
    55→    const sample = readTextSample(filePath)
    56→    if (!sample) continue
    57→
    58→    const cjkCount = (sample.match(CJK_RE) ?? []).length
    59→    const latinCount = (sample.match(LATIN_RE) ?? []).length
    60→
    61→    if (cjkCount >= 8 && cjkCount >= Math.max(4, Math.floor(latinCount / 4))) {
    62→      zhScore += cjkCount
    63→    }
    64→    if (cjkCount === 0 && latinCount >= MIN_LATIN_SIGNAL) {
    65→      enScore += Math.max(latinCount, 12)
    66→      continue
    67→    }
    68→    if (latinCount >= 40 && latinCount >= Math.max(40, cjkCount * 4)) {
    69→      enScore += latinCount
    70→    }
    71→  }
    72→
    73→  if (zhScore === 0 && enScore === 0) return null
    74→  if (zhScore === 0) return 'en'
    75→  if (enScore === 0) return 'zh-cn'
    76→  if (zhScore >= enScore * 1.25) return 'zh-cn'
    77→  if (enScore >= zhScore * 1.25) return 'en'
    78→  return null
    79→}
    80→
    81→export function detectSystemLocale(): string {
    82→  const candidates = [
    83→    process.env['LC_ALL'],
    84→    process.env['LANG'],
    85→    process.env['LANGUAGE'],
    86→  ]
    87→  for (const candidate of candidates) {
    88→    const text = (candidate ?? '').toLowerCase()
    89→    if (text.startsWith('zh') || text.includes('chinese')) {
    90→      return 'zh-cn'
    91→    }
    92→  }
    93→  return 'en'
    94→}
    95→
    96→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    97→// Internal helpers
    98→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    99→
   100→function* iterRepoTextCandidates(root: string): Generator<string> {
   101→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   102→
   103→  for (const rel of ['AGENTS.md', 'README.md', 'README.zh-CN.md', 'README.zh_CN.md']) {
   104→    const p = join(root, rel)
   105→    if (existsSync(p) && isFile(p)) {
   106→      seen.add(p)
   107→      yield p
   108→    }
   109→  }
   110→
   111→  const topLevel: string[] = []
   112→  try {
   113→    for (const entry of readdirSync(root)) {
   114→      const p = join(root, entry)
   115→      if (isFile(p) && TEXT_EXTENSIONS.has(extname(p).toLowerCase()) && !seen.has(p)) {
   116→        topLevel.push(p)
   117→      }
   118→    }
   119→  } catch {
   120→    // ignore
   121→  }
   122→  topLevel.sort()
   123→  for (const p of topLevel.slice(0, 8)) {
   124→    seen.add(p)
   125→    yield p
   126→  }
   127→
   128→  const docsDir = join(root, 'docs')
   129→  if (existsSync(docsDir) && isDir(docsDir)) {
   130→    let count = 0
   131→    for (const p of walkDir(docsDir)) {
   132→      if (count >= 12) break
   133→      if (!isFile(p) || !TEXT_EXTENSIONS.has(extname(p).toLowerCase()) || seen.has(p)) continue
   134→      seen.add(p)
   135→      count++
   136→      yield p
   137→    }
   138→  }
   139→}
   140→
   141→function walkDir(dir: string): string[] {
   142→  const results: string[] = []
   143→  try {
   144→    for (const entry of readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true })) {
   145→      const p = join(dir, entry.name)
   146→      if (entry.isDirectory()) {
   147→        results.push(...walkDir(p))
   148→      } else if (entry.isFile()) {
   149→        results.push(p)
   150→      }
   151→    }
   152→  } catch {
   153→    // ignore
   154→  }
   155→  results.sort()
   156→  return results
   157→}
   158→
   159→function readTextSample(filePath: string): string {
   160→  try {
   161→    const buf = Buffer.alloc(4096)
   162→    const fd = openSync(filePath, 'r')
   163→    const bytesRead = readSync(fd, buf, 0, 4096, 0)
   164→    closeSync(fd)
   165→    return buf.subarray(0, bytesRead).toString('utf-8')
   166→  } catch {
   167→    return ''
   168→  }
   169→}
   170→
   171→function isFile(p: string): boolean {
   172→  try { return statSync(p).isFile() } catch { return false }
   173→}
   174→
   175→function isDir(p: string): boolean {
   176→  try { return statSync(p).isDirectory() } catch { return false }
   177→}

    26→export async function cmdDiscover(options: DiscoverOptions): Promise<number> {

    31→  }
    32→
    33→  const repoSlug = slugify(options.projectName.trim() || (root.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''), 'project')
    34→  const globalRoot = options.globalRoot ? resolve(options.globalRoot) : defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
    35→  const requestedClients = options.client === 'all' ? CLIENTS : new Set([options.client])
    36→  const discovered = discoverSourceFiles(requestedClients)
    37→
    38→  const results: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
    39→  const skipped: Record<string, string>[] = []
    40→
    41→  for (const [client, source] of discovered) {
    42→    if (options.limit > 0 && results.length >= options.limit) break
    43→
    44→    let parsed
    45→    try {
    46→      parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
    47→    } catch (err: unknown) {
    48→      skipped.push({
    49→        client,
    50→        source,
    51→        reason: 'parse-error',
    52→        error: summarizeException(err),
    53→      })
    54→      continue
    55→    }
    56→
    57→    const candidateProject = inferProjectSlug(parsed)
    58→    const matchesCurrentRepo = transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, root, repoSlug)
    59→
    60→    if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) {
    61→      skipped.push({ client, source, reason: 'no-importable-content', project: candidateProject })
    62→      continue
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    if (options.scope === 'current-project' && !matchesCurrentRepo) {
    66→      skipped.push({ client, source, reason: 'unrelated-project', project: candidateProject })
    67→      continue
    68→    }
    69→
    70→    try {
    71→      const result = await importTranscript(
    72→        parsed,
    73→        root,
    74→        globalRoot,
    75→        matchesCurrentRepo ? repoSlug : candidateProject,
    76→        matchesCurrentRepo ? options.rawUploadPermission : 'not-applicable',
    77→        matchesCurrentRepo,
    78→      )
    79→      results.push({ ...result, matches_current_repo: matchesCurrentRepo })
    80→    } catch (err: unknown) {
    81→      skipped.push({
    82→        client,
    83→        source,
    84→        reason: 'import-error',
    85→        project: candidateProject,
    86→        error: summarizeException(err),
    87→      })
    88→    }
    89→  }
    90→
    91→  const payload = {
    92→    repo: toPosixPath(root),
    93→    repo_project: repoSlug,
    94→    scope: options.scope,
    95→    client_filter: options.client,
    96→    discovered_count: discovered.length,
    97→    imported_count: results.length,
    98→    repo_mirror_count: results.filter(r => r['matches_current_repo']).length,
    99→    global_only_count: results.filter(r => !r['matches_current_repo']).length,
   100→    skipped_count: skipped.length,
   101→    imports: results,
   102→    skipped,
   103→  }
   104→
   105→  if (options.format === 'json') {
   106→    process.stdout.write(JSON.stringify(payload) + '\n')
   107→  } else {
   108→    process.stdout.write(formatDiscoverText(payload) + '\n')
   109→  }
   110→  return 0
   111→}
   112→
   113→function formatDiscoverText(payload: Record<string, unknown>): string {
   114→  const lines = [
   115→    `repo: ${payload['repo'] ?? ''}`,
   116→    `repo_project: ${payload['repo_project'] ?? ''}`,
   117→    `scope: ${payload['scope'] ?? ''}`,
   118→    `client_filter: ${payload['client_filter'] ?? ''}`,
   119→    `discovered_count: ${payload['discovered_count'] ?? 0}`,
   120→    `imported_count: ${payload['imported_count'] ?? 0}`,
   121→    `repo_mirror_count: ${payload['repo_mirror_count'] ?? 0}`,
   122→    `global_only_count: ${payload['global_only_count'] ?? 0}`,
   123→    `skipped_count: ${payload['skipped_count'] ?? 0}`,
   124→  ]
   125→
   126→  const imports = payload['imports']
   127→  if (Array.isArray(imports) && imports.length > 0) {
   128→    lines.push('imports:')
   129→    for (const item of imports.slice(0, 10)) {
   130→      const rec = item as Record<string, unknown>
   131→      lines.push(`- ${rec['client']} ${rec['project']} ${rec['session_id']} repo_mirror=${String(rec['matches_current_repo']).toLowerCase()}`)
   132→    }
   133→    if (imports.length > 10) lines.push(`- ... ${imports.length - 10} more`)
   134→  }
   135→  return lines.join('\n')
   136→}
   137→
   138→function summarizeException(err: unknown): string {
   139→  if (err instanceof Error) return err.message.trim() || err.constructor.name
   140→  return String(err)
   141→}

   118→function installCron(scriptPath: string, seconds: number): number {
   119→  if (isCronRegistered()) {
   120→    process.stderr.write("Heartbeat is already registered in cron. Use 'uninstall' first.\n")
   121→    return 1
   122→  }
   123→
   124→  const minutes = Math.max(1, Math.floor(seconds / 60))
   125→  const logDir = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'logs')
   126→  mkdirSync(logDir, { recursive: true })
   127→
   128→  const cronLine = `*/${minutes} * * * * node "${scriptPath}" daemon run-once >> "${resolve(logDir, 'heartbeat-cron.log')}" 2>&1 # memorytree`
   129→  const existing = getCrontab()
   130→  const newCrontab = existing.trim()
   131→    ? existing.trimEnd() + '\n' + cronLine + '\n'
   132→    : cronLine + '\n'
   133→
   134→  try {
   135→    execCommand('crontab', ['-'], { allowFailure: false })
   136→    // Use stdin approach - write temp file and pipe
   137→    const tmpFile = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', '.crontab.tmp')
   138→    writeFileSync(tmpFile, newCrontab)
   139→    execCommand('bash', ['-c', `crontab "${tmpFile}"`])
   140→    unlinkSync(tmpFile)
   141→  } catch {
   142→    process.stderr.write('Failed to install cron job.\n')
   143→    return 1
   144→  }
   145→
   146→  process.stdout.write(`Heartbeat registered in cron (every ${minutes}m).\n`)
   147→  return 0
   148→}
   149→
   150→function uninstallCron(): number {
   151→  const existing = getCrontab()
   152→  const filtered = existing.split('\n').filter(line => !line.includes('memorytree')).join('\n') + '\n'
   153→  try {
   154→    const tmpFile = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', '.crontab.tmp')
   155→    mkdirSync(dirname(tmpFile), { recursive: true })
   156→    writeFileSync(tmpFile, filtered)
   157→    execCommand('bash', ['-c', `crontab "${tmpFile}"`])
   158→    unlinkSync(tmpFile)
   159→  } catch {
   160→    // best effort
   161→  }
   162→  process.stdout.write('Heartbeat removed from cron.\n')
   163→  return 0
   164→}
   165→
   166→export function isCronRegistered(): boolean {
   167→  return getCrontab().includes('memorytree')

   186→function installLaunchd(scriptPath: string, seconds: number): number {
   187→  const plistPath = launchdPlistPath()

   189→    process.stderr.write("Heartbeat plist already exists. Use 'uninstall' first.\n")
   190→    return 1
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  const logDir = resolve(homedir(), '.memorytree', 'logs')
   194→  mkdirSync(logDir, { recursive: true })
   195→
   196→  const plistContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
   197→<!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC "-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN" "http://www.apple.com/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd">
   198→<plist version="1.0">
   199→<dict>
   200→    <key>Label</key>
   201→    <string>${LAUNCHD_LABEL}</string>
   202→    <key>ProgramArguments</key>
   203→    <array>
   204→        <string>node</string>
   205→        <string>${scriptPath}</string>
   206→        <string>daemon</string>
   207→        <string>run-once</string>
   208→    </array>
   209→    <key>StartInterval</key>
   210→    <integer>${seconds}</integer>
   211→    <key>StandardOutPath</key>
   212→    <string>${resolve(logDir, 'heartbeat-launchd.log')}</string>
   213→    <key>StandardErrorPath</key>
   214→    <string>${resolve(logDir, 'heartbeat-launchd.log')}</string>
   215→</dict>
   216→</plist>
   217→`
   218→  mkdirSync(dirname(plistPath), { recursive: true })
   219→  writeFileSync(plistPath, plistContent, 'utf-8')
   220→
   221→  try {
   222→    execCommand('launchctl', ['load', plistPath])
   223→  } catch {
   224→    process.stderr.write('Failed to load plist.\n')
   225→    return 1
   226→  }
   227→
   228→  process.stdout.write(`Heartbeat registered via launchd (every ${seconds}s).\n`)
   229→  return 0
   230→}
   231→
   232→function uninstallLaunchd(): number {
   233→  const plistPath = launchdPlistPath()
   234→  if (existsSync(plistPath)) {
   235→    try { execCommand('launchctl', ['unload', plistPath], { allowFailure: true }) } catch { /* ignore */ }
   236→    try { unlinkSync(plistPath) } catch { /* ignore */ }
   237→  }
   238→  process.stdout.write('Heartbeat removed from launchd.\n')
   239→  return 0
   240→}
   241→
   242→export function isLaunchdRegistered(): boolean {
   243→  return existsSync(launchdPlistPath())

   246→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

   250→function installSchtasks(scriptPath: string, seconds: number): number {
   251→  if (isSchtasksRegistered()) {

   263→    ])
   264→  } catch {

   266→    return 1
   267→  }
   268→
   269→  process.stdout.write(`Heartbeat registered in Task Scheduler (every ${minutes}m).\n`)
   270→  return 0
   271→}

   273→function uninstallSchtasks(): number {
   274→  try {
   275→    execCommand('schtasks', ['/delete', '/tn', TASK_NAME, '/f'], { allowFailure: true })
   276→  } catch {
   277→    // best effort
   278→  }
   279→  process.stdout.write('Heartbeat removed from Task Scheduler.\n')
   280→  return 0
   281→}

   283→export function isSchtasksRegistered(): boolean {
   284→  try {
   285→    execCommand('schtasks', ['/query', '/tn', TASK_NAME])
   286→    return true
   287→  } catch {
   288→    return false
   289→  }
   290→}

    30→export function cmdInit(options: InitOptions): number {

    35→  }

    43→  }
    44→
    45→  const agentsPath = join(root, 'AGENTS.md')
    46→  if (existsSync(agentsPath)) {

    57→      `External repo policy files detected (${preview}). ` +
    58→      'Use memorytree upgrade to preserve host commit and PR rules.\n',
    59→    )
    60→    return 1
    61→  }
    62→
    63→  const skillRoot = resolve(new URL(import.meta.url).pathname.replace(/^\/([A-Z]:)/, '$1'), '..', '..', '..')

    65→  const dt = buildDatetime(options.date, options.time)
    66→

    69→  scaffoldContentFiles(paths, templates, options.goalSummary, options.projectName, options.force)

    71→

    17→  client: string
    18→  projectName: string
    19→  globalRoot: string
    20→  rawUploadPermission: string
    21→  format: string
    22→}
    23→
    24→export async function cmdImport(options: ImportOptions): Promise<number> {
    25→  const root = resolve(options.root)
    26→  const source = resolve(options.source)
    27→
    28→  if (!existsSync(root)) {
    29→    process.stderr.write(`root does not exist: ${root}\n`)
    30→    return 1
    31→  }
    32→  if (!existsSync(source)) {
    33→    process.stderr.write(`source transcript does not exist: ${source}\n`)
    34→    return 1
    35→  }
    36→
    37→  const client = inferClient(options.client, source)
    38→  const globalRoot = options.globalRoot ? resolve(options.globalRoot) : defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
    39→  const repoSlug = slugify(options.projectName.trim() || (root.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''), 'project')
    40→
    41→  const parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
    42→  if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) {
    43→    process.stderr.write(`source transcript does not contain any importable messages or tool events: ${source}\n`)
    44→    return 1
    45→  }
    46→
    47→  const detectedProject = inferProjectSlug(parsed)
    48→  const matchesCurrentRepo = transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, root, repoSlug)
    49→
    50→  const result = await importTranscript(
    51→    parsed,
    52→    root,
    53→    globalRoot,
    54→    matchesCurrentRepo ? repoSlug : detectedProject,
    55→    matchesCurrentRepo ? options.rawUploadPermission : 'not-applicable',
    56→    matchesCurrentRepo,
    57→  )
    58→
    59→  const output = {
    60→    ...result,
    61→    matches_current_repo: matchesCurrentRepo,
    62→    detected_project: detectedProject,
    63→  } as Record<string, unknown>
    64→
    65→  if (options.format === 'json') {
    66→    process.stdout.write(JSON.stringify(output) + '\n')
    67→  } else {
    68→    process.stdout.write(formatImportText(output) + '\n')
    69→  }
    70→  return 0
    71→}
    72→
    73→function formatImportText(result: Record<string, unknown>): string {
    74→  return [
    75→    `client: ${result['client'] ?? ''}`,
    76→    `project: ${result['project'] ?? ''}`,
    77→    `session_id: ${result['session_id'] ?? ''}`,
    78→    `started_at: ${result['started_at'] ?? ''}`,
    79→    `detected_project: ${result['detected_project'] ?? ''}`,
    80→    `matches_current_repo: ${String(result['matches_current_repo'] ?? false).toLowerCase()}`,
    81→    `raw_upload_permission: ${result['raw_upload_permission'] ?? ''}`,
    82→    `message_count: ${result['message_count'] ?? 0}`,
    83→    `tool_event_count: ${result['tool_event_count'] ?? 0}`,
    84→    `repo_raw_path: ${result['repo_raw_path'] ?? ''}`,
    85→    `repo_clean_path: ${result['repo_clean_path'] ?? ''}`,
    86→    `repo_manifest_path: ${result['repo_manifest_path'] ?? ''}`,
    87→    `global_raw_path: ${result['global_raw_path'] ?? ''}`,
    88→    `global_clean_path: ${result['global_clean_path'] ?? ''}`,
    89→  ].join('\n')
    90→}

    24→export function detectState(root: string): string {
    25→  const memoryDir = join(root, 'Memory')
    26→  const goalDir = join(root, 'Memory', '01_goals')
    27→  const todoDir = join(root, 'Memory', '02_todos')
    28→  const chatDir = join(root, 'Memory', '03_chat_logs')
    29→  const agentsPath = join(root, 'AGENTS.md')
    30→  const policySources = findExternalPolicySources(root)
    31→
    32→  const latestGoal = findLatestGoalFile(goalDir)
    33→  const goalVersion = extractGoalVersion(latestGoal)
    34→  const hasGoal = latestGoal !== null
    35→  const hasTodo = goalVersion !== null && findLatestTodoFile(todoDir, goalVersion) !== null
    36→  const hasChat = findLatestChatLogFile(chatDir) !== null
    37→  const hasAgents = existsSync(agentsPath) && isFile(agentsPath)
    38→  const agentsReady = hasAgents && !needsAgentsMerge(agentsPath)
    39→
    40→  if (!existsSync(memoryDir)) {
    41→    return (hasAgents || policySources.length > 0) ? 'partial' : 'not-installed'
    42→  }
    43→  if (hasGoal && hasTodo && hasChat && agentsReady) {
    44→    return 'installed'
    45→  }
    46→  return 'partial'
    47→}

    49→export function extractGoalVersion(filePath: string | null): string | null {
    50→  if (filePath === null) return null

    52→  const match = /^goal_v(\d{3})_\d{8}\.md$/.exec(name)
    53→  return match?.[1] ?? null

   189→export interface UpgradeResult {
   190→  state_before: string
   191→  state_after: string
   192→  requested_locale: string
   193→  effective_locale: string
   194→  created_dirs: string[]
   195→  created_files: string[]
   196→  preserved_files: string[]
   197→  agents_action: string
   198→  agents_merge_required: boolean
   199→}
   200→
   201→export function upgrade(
   202→  root: string,
   203→  skillRoot: string,
   204→  templates: string,
   205→  effectiveLocale: string,
   206→  requestedLocale: string,
   207→  goalSummary: string,
   208→  projectName: string,
   209→  dt: Date,
   210→): UpgradeResult {
   211→  const initialState = detectState(root)
   212→
   213→  const createdDirs = createMemoryDirs(root)
   214→  const paths = resolveScaffoldPaths(root, dt)
   215→  const { created: createdFiles, preserved: preservedFiles } = scaffoldContentFiles(
   216→    paths, templates, goalSummary, projectName, false,
   217→  )
   218→
   219→  const agentsPath = join(root, 'AGENTS.md')
   220→  let agentsAction = 'preserved_existing'
   221→  if (!existsSync(agentsPath)) {
   222→    const agentsTemplate = join(templates, 'agents.md')
   223→    if (existsSync(agentsTemplate) && writeTemplate(agentsTemplate, agentsPath, false, {})) {
   224→      createdFiles.push('AGENTS.md')
   225→      agentsAction = 'created'
   226→    }
   227→  } else {
   228→    preservedFiles.push('AGENTS.md')
   229→  }
   230→  const mergeRequired = agentsAction === 'preserved_existing' && needsAgentsMerge(agentsPath)
   231→
   232→  return {
   233→    state_before: initialState,
   234→    state_after: detectState(root),
   235→    requested_locale: requestedLocale,
   236→    effective_locale: effectiveLocale,
   237→    created_dirs: createdDirs,
   238→    created_files: createdFiles,
   239→    preserved_files: preservedFiles,
   240→    agents_action: agentsAction,
   241→    agents_merge_required: mergeRequired,
   242→  }
   243→}
   244→
   245→export function formatResultText(result: UpgradeResult): string {
   246→  const lines = [
   247→    `state_before: ${result.state_before}`,
   248→    `state_after: ${result.state_after}`,
   249→    `effective_locale: ${result.effective_locale}`,
   250→    `agents_action: ${result.agents_action}`,
   251→    `agents_merge_required: ${result.agents_merge_required}`,
   252→  ]
   253→  if (result.created_dirs.length > 0) {
   254→    lines.push('created_dirs:')
   255→    for (const item of result.created_dirs) lines.push(`- ${item}`)
   256→  }
   257→  if (result.created_files.length > 0) {
   258→    lines.push('created_files:')
   259→    for (const item of result.created_files) lines.push(`- ${item}`)
   260→  }
   261→  if (result.preserved_files.length > 0) {
   262→    lines.push('preserved_files:')
   263→    for (const item of result.preserved_files) lines.push(`- ${item}`)
   264→  }
   265→  return lines.join('\n')
   266→}

    21→export interface RecallResult {
    22→  found: boolean

    24→  repo: string
    25→  imported_count: number
    26→  message?: string
    27→  client?: string
    28→  session_id?: string
    29→  title?: string
    30→  started_at?: string
    31→  cwd?: string

    39→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    40→// Public API
    41→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    42→
    43→export async function recall(
    44→  root: string,
    45→  projectName: string,
    46→  globalRootOverride: string,
    47→  activationTime: string,
    48→): Promise<RecallResult> {
    49→  const resolvedRoot = resolve(root)
    50→  const repoSlug = slugify(projectName.trim() || (resolvedRoot.split(/[/\\]/).pop() ?? ''), 'project')
    51→  const globalRoot = globalRootOverride ? resolve(globalRootOverride) : defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
    52→  const effectiveActivation = activationTime || nowIso()
    53→
    54→  const imported = await syncCurrentProject(resolvedRoot, repoSlug, globalRoot)
    55→
    56→  const session = await findLatestSession(globalRoot, resolvedRoot, repoSlug, effectiveActivation)
    57→
    58→  if (session === null) {
    59→    return {
    60→      found: false,
    61→      project: repoSlug,
    62→      repo: toPosixPath(resolvedRoot),
    63→      imported_count: imported,
    64→      message: 'No previous session found for this project.',
    65→    }
    66→  }
    67→
    68→  const cleanPath = String(session['global_clean_path'] ?? '')
    69→  let cleanContent = ''
    70→  if (cleanPath && existsSync(cleanPath)) {
    71→    try {
    72→      cleanContent = readFileSync(cleanPath, 'utf-8')
    73→    } catch {
    74→      // ignore read errors
    75→    }
    76→  }
    77→
    78→  return {
    79→    found: true,
    80→    project: repoSlug,
    81→    repo: toPosixPath(resolvedRoot),
    82→    imported_count: imported,
    83→    client: String(session['client'] ?? ''),
    84→    session_id: String(session['session_id'] ?? ''),
    85→    title: String(session['title'] ?? ''),
    86→    started_at: String(session['started_at'] ?? ''),
    87→    cwd: String(session['cwd'] ?? ''),
    88→    branch: String(session['branch'] ?? ''),
    89→    message_count: Number(session['message_count'] ?? 0),
    90→    tool_event_count: Number(session['tool_event_count'] ?? 0),
    91→    global_clean_path: cleanPath,
    92→    clean_content: cleanContent,
    93→  }
    94→}
    95→
    96→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    97→// Sync current project
    98→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    99→
   100→export async function syncCurrentProject(root: string, repoSlug: string, globalRoot: string): Promise<number> {
   101→  const discovered = discoverSourceFiles()
   102→  let imported = 0
   103→
   104→  for (const [client, source] of discovered) {
   105→    let parsed
   106→    try {
   107→      parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
   108→    } catch {
   109→      continue
   110→    }
   111→
   112→    if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) continue
   113→    if (!transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, root, repoSlug)) continue
   114→
   115→    try {
   116→      await importTranscript(parsed, root, globalRoot, repoSlug, 'not-set', true)
   117→      imported++
   118→    } catch {
   119→      continue
   120→    }
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  return imported
   124→}
   125→
   126→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   127→// Find latest session
   128→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   129→
   130→export async function findLatestSession(
   131→  globalRoot: string,
   132→  root: string,
   133→  repoSlug: string,
   134→  activationTime: string,
   135→): Promise<Record<string, unknown> | null> {
   136→  const dbPath = join(globalRoot, 'index', 'search.sqlite')
   137→  if (!existsSync(dbPath)) {
   138→    return findLatestFromJsonl(globalRoot, root, repoSlug, activationTime)
   139→  }
   140→
   141→  try {
   142→    const SQL = await initSqlJs()
   143→    const db = new SQL.Database(readFileSync(dbPath))
   144→    try {
   145→      const stmt = db.prepare(
   146→        'SELECT * FROM transcripts WHERE started_at < ? ORDER BY started_at DESC LIMIT 20',
   147→      )
   148→      stmt.bind([activationTime])
   149→
   150→      const resolvedRoot = toPosixPath(resolve(root)).toLowerCase()
   151→      const columns = stmt.getColumnNames()
   152→
   153→      while (stmt.step()) {
   154→        const values = stmt.get()
   155→        const row: Record<string, unknown> = {}
   156→        for (let i = 0; i < columns.length; i++) {
   157→          row[columns[i]!] = values[i]
   158→        }
   159→        const cwd = String(row['cwd'] ?? '')
   160→        const project = String(row['project'] ?? '')
   161→        if (cwdMatches(cwd, resolvedRoot) || project === repoSlug) {
   162→          stmt.free()
   163→          return row
   164→        }
   165→      }
   166→      stmt.free()
   167→    } finally {
   168→      db.close()
   169→    }
   170→  } catch {
   171→    return findLatestFromJsonl(globalRoot, root, repoSlug, activationTime)
   172→  }
   173→
   174→  return null
   175→}
   176→
   177→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   178→// JSONL fallback
   179→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   180→
   181→export function findLatestFromJsonl(
   182→  globalRoot: string,
   183→  root: string,
   184→  repoSlug: string,
   185→  activationTime: string,
   186→): Record<string, unknown> | null {
   187→  const jsonlPath = join(globalRoot, 'index', 'sessions.jsonl')
   188→  if (!existsSync(jsonlPath)) return null
   189→
   190→  const resolvedRoot = toPosixPath(resolve(root)).toLowerCase()
   191→  const candidates: Record<string, unknown>[] = []
   192→
   193→  let content: string
   194→  try {
   195→    content = readFileSync(jsonlPath, 'utf-8')
   196→  } catch {
   197→    return null
   198→  }
   199→
   200→  for (const line of content.split('\n')) {
   201→    const trimmed = line.trim()
   202→    if (!trimmed) continue
   203→    let entry: Record<string, unknown>
   204→    try {
   205→      entry = JSON.parse(trimmed) as Record<string, unknown>
   206→    } catch {
   207→      continue
   208→    }
   209→
   210→    const started = String(entry['started_at'] ?? '')
   211→    if (started >= activationTime) continue
   212→
   213→    const cwd = String(entry['cwd'] ?? '')
   214→    const project = String(entry['project'] ?? '')
   215→    if (cwdMatches(cwd, resolvedRoot) || project === repoSlug) {
   216→      candidates.push(entry)
   217→    }
   218→  }
   219→
   220→  if (candidates.length === 0) return null
   221→
   222→  candidates.sort((a, b) => {
   223→    const aTime = String(a['started_at'] ?? '')
   224→    const bTime = String(b['started_at'] ?? '')
   225→    return bTime.localeCompare(aTime)
   226→  })
   227→  return candidates[0]!
   228→}
   229→
   230→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   231→// CWD matching
   232→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   233→
   234→export function cwdMatches(cwd: string, resolvedRoot: string): boolean {
   235→  if (!cwd) return false
   236→  try {
   237→    const cwdResolved = toPosixPath(resolve(cwd)).toLowerCase()
   238→    if (cwdResolved === resolvedRoot) return true
   239→    const prefix = resolvedRoot.endsWith('/') ? resolvedRoot : resolvedRoot + '/'
   240→    return cwdResolved.startsWith(prefix)
   241→  } catch {
   242→    return false
   243→  }
   244→}
   245→
   246→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   247→// Helpers
   248→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   249→
   250→function nowIso(): string {
   251→  return new Date().toISOString().replace(/\.\d{3}Z$/, 'Z')
   252→}
   253→
   254→export function formatText(payload: RecallResult): string {
   255→  if (!payload.found) {
   256→    return [
   257→      `project: ${payload.project}`,
   258→      `imported: ${payload.imported_count}`,
   259→      `result: ${payload.message ?? 'No previous session found.'}`,
   260→    ].join('\n')
   261→  }
   262→
   263→  const lines = [
   264→    `project: ${payload.project}`,
   265→    `client: ${payload.client ?? ''}`,
   266→    `session_id: ${payload.session_id ?? ''}`,
   267→    `title: ${payload.title ?? ''}`,
   268→    `started_at: ${payload.started_at ?? ''}`,
   269→    `cwd: ${payload.cwd ?? ''}`,
   270→    `branch: ${payload.branch ?? ''}`,
   271→    `messages: ${payload.message_count ?? 0}`,
   272→    `tool_events: ${payload.tool_event_count ?? 0}`,
   273→    `imported_this_sync: ${payload.imported_count}`,
   274→    `clean_transcript: ${payload.global_clean_path ?? ''}`,
   275→  ]
   276→
   277→  if (payload.clean_content) {
   278→    lines.push('', '--- clean transcript content ---', payload.clean_content)
   279→  }
   280→
   281→  return lines.join('\n')
   282→}

    87→

   167→
   168→    await upsertSearchIndex(dbPath, m1)
   169→    await upsertSearchIndex(dbPath, m2)
   170→    await upsertSearchIndex(dbPath, m3)
   171→
   172→    const SQL = await initSqlJs()
   173→    const db = new SQL.Database(readFileSync(dbPath))
   174→    try {
   175→      const rows = db.exec('SELECT * FROM transcripts ORDER BY session_id')
   176→      expect(rows).toHaveLength(1)
   177→      expect(rows[0]!.values).toHaveLength(3)
   178→

   180→      const sessionIdx = columns.indexOf('session_id')
   181→      expect(rows[0]!.values[0]![sessionIdx]).toBe('sess-001')
   182→      expect(rows[0]!.values[1]![sessionIdx]).toBe('sess-002')
   183→      expect(rows[0]!.values[2]![sessionIdx]).toBe('sess-003')
   184→    } finally {
   185→      db.close()
   186→    }
   187→  })

   195→

   485→  })

   487→    expect(extractSimpleText(null)).toBe('')
   488→  })
   489→  it('returns empty for number', () => {
   490→    expect(extractSimpleText(42)).toBe('')
   491→  })

   526→  })

   529→  })

   531→    const val = { parts: [{ text: 'a' }], content: [{ text: 'b' }] }
   532→    expect(extractGeminiParts(val)).toEqual(['a', 'b'])
   533→  })

   536→  })

   586→    ]

   594→    ]

   602→    ]
   603→    expect(deduplicateMessages(messages)).toHaveLength(2)
   604→  })
   605→

   609→      { role: 'user', text: 'hello', timestamp: null },
   610→    ]

   612→  })

   616→  })

   309→    utimesSync(older, olderTime, olderTime)

    40→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    41→// Helpers
    42→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    43→
    44→function findLogFile(): string | undefined {
    45→  const logsDir = join(tmpDir, '.memorytree', 'logs')
    46→  try {
    47→    const files = readdirSync(logsDir)
    48→    return files.find(f => f.startsWith('heartbeat-') && f.endsWith('.log'))
    49→  } catch {
    50→    return undefined
    51→  }
    52→}
    53→
    54→function readLogContents(): string {
    55→  const logsDir = join(tmpDir, '.memorytree', 'logs')
    56→  const file = findLogFile()
    57→  if (!file) return ''
    58→  return readFileSync(join(logsDir, file), 'utf-8')
    59→}

    55→    expect(path.startsWith(tmpDir)).toBe(true)

    59→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    60→// acquireLock / releaseLock
    61→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    62→
    63→describe('acquireLock / releaseLock', () => {
    64→  it('acquireLock succeeds when no lock exists', () => {
    65→    expect(acquireLock()).toBe(true)
    66→  })
    67→
    68→  it('acquireLock fails when lock is held by current process', () => {
    69→    expect(acquireLock()).toBe(true)
    70→    // Second acquire should fail because current PID is alive
    71→    expect(acquireLock()).toBe(false)
    72→  })
    73→
    74→  it('releaseLock removes the lock file', () => {
    75→    acquireLock()
    76→    releaseLock()
    77→    expect(existsSync(lockPath())).toBe(false)
    78→  })
    79→
    80→  it('acquire succeeds after release', () => {
    81→    expect(acquireLock()).toBe(true)
    82→    releaseLock()
    83→    expect(acquireLock()).toBe(true)
    84→  })
    85→})
    86→
    87→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    88→// readLockPid
    89→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    90→
    91→describe('readLockPid', () => {
    92→  it('returns PID when lock is held', () => {
    93→    acquireLock()
    94→    const pid = readLockPid()
    95→    expect(pid).toBe(process.pid)
    96→  })
    97→
    98→  it('returns null when no lock file exists', () => {
    99→    expect(readLockPid()).toBeNull()
   100→  })
   101→
   102→  it('returns null for corrupt lock file', () => {
   103→    const path = lockPath()
   104→    mkdirSync(join(tmpDir, '.memorytree'), { recursive: true })
   105→    writeFileSync(path, 'not-a-number')
   106→    expect(readLockPid()).toBeNull()

   148→  })
   149→

   154→
   155→    expect(acquireLock()).toBe(true)

   225→      return true
   226→    }) as typeof process.stderr.write
   227→    process.stdout.write = ((chunk: string) => {
   228→      stdoutChunks.push(chunk)
   229→      return true
   230→    }) as typeof process.stdout.write
   231→

   233→    // On any supported platform it returns 0; unsupported returns 1

# Second-Round Security and Consistency Review

## 1. SECURITY REVIEW

### 1.1 SQL Injection in src/transcript/db.ts

Rating: OK (No Issue)

db.ts:84-90 builds the UPSERT statement with ? placeholders and passes values via a params array (line 126: db.run(UPSERT_SQL, params)). The column names in ALL_COLUMNS are static string literals defined at module scope (lines 30-52), not derived from user input. The CREATE_TABLE_SQL is also a static string. Parameters are properly bound. No injection vector exists.

### 1.2 Command Injection in src/utils/exec.ts

Rating: OK (No Issue)

exec.ts:23 uses execFileSync(command, [...args]), which is the safe variant that does not invoke a shell. Arguments are passed as an array, preventing shell metacharacter injection. The command parameter is always a hardcoded string ('git', 'tasklist', 'crontab', 'schtasks', 'launchctl'), never user-supplied.

Rating: MEDIUM -- One exception at src/cli/cmd-daemon.ts:139:

execCommand('bash', ['-c', `crontab "${tmpFile}"`])

This uses bash -c which re-introduces shell interpretation. If tmpFile contained shell metacharacters (e.g., if the homedir contained $(...) or backticks), this could be exploited. The tmpFile path is derived from homedir() which is OS-controlled, making exploitation unlikely but not impossible. The same pattern appears at line 157.

File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\cli\cmd-daemon.ts lines 139, 157

Recommendation: Replace bash -c with a direct crontab call using stdin piping, or use execFileSync('crontab', [tmpFile]) directly.

### 1.3 Path Traversal in import/discover/scaffold

Rating: LOW

- cmd-import.ts:25-26 uses resolve(options.root) and resolve(options.source) which normalizes .. segments. However, there is no containment check verifying that the resolved source path does not escape outside the intended directories.
- scaffold.ts:102-109 (resolveTemplateDir) uses join(skillRoot, 'assets', 'templates', localeName). If localeName contained ../.., it could escape the templates directory. The normalizeLocale function (locale.ts:22-41) normalizes to known values or passes through unknown values unchanged. A locale like ../../etc would pass through as-is.

File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\project\scaffold.ts line 105
File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\project\locale.ts line 40

Recommendation: Validate that localeName matches /^[a-z]{2}(-[a-z]{2})?$/ before using it in path construction, or verify the resolved template directory is a child of templatesRoot.

### 1.4 Sensitive Data in Logs

Rating: OK (No Issue)

heartbeat.ts:145-146 logs only metadata about sensitive detections ("Sensitive pattern detected in transcript {source_path}"), never the matched content itself. The scanSensitive function correctly writes the alert with just the filename basename, not the sensitive value. The log.ts logger does not inject any ambient sensitive data.

### 1.5 Lock File Race Conditions (TOCTOU) in lock.ts

Rating: LOW

The acquireLock() function at lock.ts:42-83 has a two-phase approach:
1. Phase 1 (lines 46-69): Checks if lock file exists, reads PID, checks if process is alive, removes stale lock.
2. Phase 2 (lines 72-81): Creates lock file with O_CREAT | O_EXCL.

There is a TOCTOU window between removing the stale lock (line 61 or 67) and creating the new lock (line 73). Two processes could both detect the stale lock, both remove it, and then both attempt O_CREAT | O_EXCL. However, only one will succeed because O_EXCL is atomic at the filesystem level. The losing process falls through to the catch block (line 77) and returns false. This is correctly handled.

The comment at line 71 ("Use exclusive create to prevent TOCTOU race") is accurate. The design is sound.

### 1.6 Config TOML Injection

Rating: MEDIUM

config.ts:82 constructs TOML by string interpolation:

const items = cfg.watch_dirs.map(d => `"${d}"`).join(', ')

If a watch_dirs entry contains a double quote or backslash, the generated TOML will be malformed or could inject additional TOML keys. Similarly, config.ts:91-92:

lines.push(`path = "${project.path}"`)
lines.push(`name = "${project.name}"`)

Neither project.path nor project.name are escaped for TOML string syntax.

File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\heartbeat\config.ts lines 82, 91-92

Recommendation: Escape double quotes and backslashes in TOML string values before interpolation, or use a TOML serialization library.

### 1.7 Launchd Plist XML Injection

Rating: MEDIUM

cmd-daemon.ts:196-217 builds a plist XML string by interpolating scriptPath and logDir values directly into XML without escaping <, >, &, or ". If the script path or log directory contains XML special characters, the plist will be malformed or could inject arbitrary XML elements.

File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\cli\cmd-daemon.ts lines 196-217

Recommendation: XML-escape the interpolated values, or use a proper plist builder.

---

## 2. CROSS-MODULE CONSISTENCY

### 2.1 toPosixPath Usage for Persistent Writes

Rating: OK (Mostly Consistent)

Reviewed all modules that write paths to files:

- import.ts:74-81: Uses toPosixPath() for all stored paths (raw_source_path, repo_raw_path, repo_clean_path, repo_manifest_path, global_raw_path, global_clean_path).
- discover.ts:38,73: Uses toPosixPath() for defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot() and discovered file paths.
- config.ts:124: Uses toPosixPath() for registerProject path storage.
- heartbeat.ts:82-84,149,184,192,197: Uses toPosixPath() for all alert project keys.
- scaffold.ts:122,129,311,365,367: Uses toPosixPath() for policy source paths and created dir/file listings.
- recall.ts:63,82,150,190: Uses toPosixPath() for resolvedRoot in display and cwd matching.

One inconsistency found:

Rating: LOW -- import.ts:41-43 builds repo paths with join() (which uses backslashes on Windows) for the raw repoRawPath, repoCleanPath, repoManifestPath variables. These are later converted via toPosixPath(relative(root, repoRawPath)) at line 77, so the final stored value is posix. However, the local paths used for file operations (e.g., copyFile(parsed.source_path, repoRawPath) at line 62) use native OS paths, which is correct for I/O. No actual bug here.

### 2.2 normalizeTimestamp Consistency

Rating: OK (Consistent)

- import.ts:29: Uses normalizeTimestamp(new Date()) for importedAt.
- parse.ts:76,84,184,192,282,299,322: Uses normalizeTimestamp() for all timestamp fields in all three parsers.
- alert.ts:54-56: Has its own utcTimestamp() function that produces new Date().toISOString().replace(/\.\d{3}Z$/, 'Z').

Rating: LOW -- alert.ts uses its own utcTimestamp() (line 54) rather than the shared normalizeTimestamp(). The output format differs slightly: utcTimestamp() strips milliseconds from toISOString() (producing 2024-01-01T00:00:00Z), while normalizeTimestamp(new Date()) uses formatUtcIso() (common.ts:327-334) which also produces YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ. The formats are functionally equivalent, but having two implementations for the same purpose creates maintenance risk.

File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\heartbeat\alert.ts line 54

### 2.3 ManifestEntry Field Consistency

Rating: HIGH

There is a field mismatch between ManifestEntry in types/transcript.ts and the SQLite schema in db.ts:

types/transcript.ts defines ManifestEntry with 20 fields:
- global_manifest_path (line 43)
- cleaning_mode (line 49)
- repo_mirror_enabled (line 50)

db.ts defines 18 columns (lines 30-52). The DATA_COLUMNS and PK_COLUMNS arrays total 18 columns. The following fields from ManifestEntry are not in the SQLite schema:
- global_manifest_path
- cleaning_mode
- repo_mirror_enabled

At db.ts:117-124, the code maps ALL_COLUMNS to values from the manifest record. Since ALL_COLUMNS only has 18 entries, the three extra ManifestEntry fields are silently dropped. This is likely intentional (the SQLite index doesn't need these fields), but the db test at db.test.ts:15-37 constructs its makeManifest() without global_manifest_path, cleaning_mode, or repo_mirror_enabled -- it does not include these fields, yet passes the typecheck because makeManifest returns ManifestEntry using a spread. This means the test helper is technically missing required fields from the type.

File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\transcript\db.ts lines 30-52 vs D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\src\types\transcript.ts lines 29-51
File: D:\demo1\memorytree-workflow\tests\transcript\db.test.ts lines 15-37

Recommendation: Either add the three missing columns to the SQLite schema, or create a narrower type (e.g., SearchIndexEntry) that omits the fields not stored in SQLite, and use that as the parameter type for upsertSearchIndex().

### 2.4 Barrel Export in transcript/index.ts

Rating: OK (Complete)

The barrel export at src/transcript/index.ts re-exports everything from:
- common.ts: All 22 public functions/constants
- parse.ts: All 5 public functions
- db.ts: upsertSearchIndex
- discover.ts: All 7 public functions
- import.ts: All 8 public functions
- Types from types/transcript.ts: All 5 types

All public symbols from each module are accounted for. No missing exports.

## 3. TEST COVERAGE GAPS

### 3.1 Functions Without Test Coverage

Rating: HIGH -- The following exported functions have no direct tests:

1. src/heartbeat/heartbeat.ts: main(), runHeartbeat(), processProject(), gitCommitAndPush(), tryPush() -- These are the core heartbeat orchestration functions. Only scanSensitive() is tested. The Python codebase had integration-level tests for these; the TS port does not.

2. src/recall/recall.ts: recall(), syncCurrentProject(), findLatestSession() (the SQLite path) -- Only cwdMatches(), findLatestFromJsonl(), and formatText() are tested. The main recall() function and the SQLite query path in findLatestSession() have no tests.

3. src/cli/cmd-init.ts: cmdInit() -- No test file exists for this command handler.

4. src/cli/cmd-import.ts: cmdImport() -- No test file exists.

5. src/cli/cmd-discover.ts: cmdDiscover() -- No test file exists.

6. src/cli/cmd-upgrade.ts: cmdUpgrade() -- No test file exists.

7. src/cli/cmd-locale.ts: cmdLocale() -- No test file exists.

8. src/cli/cmd-recall.ts: cmdRecall() -- No test file exists.

9. src/cli/cmd-daemon.ts: cmdWatch(), installCron(), installLaunchd(), installSchtasks() -- Only cmdInstall() config-saving is tested; the actual scheduler registration logic is not tested.

10. src/project/upgrade.ts: upgrade() is tested but formatResultText() edge cases (e.g., all lists populated) are minimal.

### 3.2 Edge Cases Not Covered

Rating: MEDIUM

1. Unicode paths: No test verifies that file operations work correctly with Unicode characters in file paths (e.g., CJK directory names). The slugify() function is tested with non-ASCII, but actual filesystem operations with Unicode paths are not.

2. Empty/corrupt SQLite database: db.ts reads an existing database at line 110. No test verifies behavior when the file exists but contains corrupt data (e.g., truncated file, wrong format).

3. Concurrent access to alerts.json: alert.ts uses a read-then-write pattern (readAlerts() then saveAlerts()) with no file locking. Two concurrent heartbeat processes could lose alert data. No test covers this.

4. Windows path edge cases in heartbeatScriptPath(): cmd-daemon.ts:298 uses import.meta.url parsing with a regex to strip the leading slash on Windows drive letters. This is fragile and not tested on actual Windows drive paths with spaces.

5. resolveTemplateDir with missing templates: Tested implicitly but no direct test for the error thrown when existsSync(templateDir) returns false.

### 3.3 Test Isolation

Rating: OK (Good)

All test files properly use mkdtempSync() / rmSync() for temp directory lifecycle. Heartbeat/alert/config/lock/log tests mock homedir() to point to temp directories, preventing pollution of the real home directory. The logger singleton is properly reset between tests via _resetLogger(). No global state leaks detected.

## 4. API CONTRACT

### 4.1 CLI Output Format Compatibility

Rating: MEDIUM

The text output formats differ slightly from what a Python CLI might produce:

1. cmd-discover.ts:131: Outputs repo_mirror=true/false as lowercase string. This matches typical JSON boolean serialization.

2. cmd-import.ts:80: Outputs matches_current_repo: true/false as lowercase.

3. cmd-recall.ts: The formatText() output uses imported_this_sync (recall.ts:273) rather than imported_count. The JSON output uses imported_count (from RecallResult). This is consistent within the TS codebase but may differ from the Python CLI if it used a different field name.

4. JSON output: All commands serialize via JSON.stringify(payload) + '\n', producing compact JSON on a single line. The Python scripts likely used json.dumps() which by default also produces compact JSON. This should be compatible.

### 4.2 Commander Options Registration

Rating: OK (Complete)

All subcommands match the expected CLI interface from SKILL.md:
- init, upgrade, import, discover, locale, recall -- all registered with correct options
- daemon install|uninstall|run-once|watch|status -- all registered as sub-subcommands

One note: main.ts:196 registers --interval for daemon watch but does not validate the format. Invalid intervals silently fall back to the default (300 seconds). This matches the Python behavior.

### 4.3 SKILL.md References

Rating: OK

SKILL.md was reviewed in full. Key findings:

- Line 109: references/execution-environment.md says "requires Node.js >= 20" -- this is correct for the TS migration.
- Line 26: Says "memorytree init" and "memorytree upgrade" -- references the memorytree CLI name which matches main.ts:11.
- No remaining Python-specific references (e.g., no mention of python, uv run, or .py scripts).
- Line 113: Lists CLI commands: memorytree init, memorytree upgrade, memorytree import, memorytree discover, memorytree locale, memorytree recall, memorytree daemon install|uninstall|run-once|watch|status -- all of these are registered in main.ts.

## SUMMARY OF FINDINGS

### CRITICAL (0)

None.

### HIGH (2)

1. ManifestEntry/SQLite schema mismatch (db.ts vs types/transcript.ts): Three fields in ManifestEntry (global_manifest_path, cleaning_mode, repo_mirror_enabled) are silently dropped when writing to SQLite. The test helper makeManifest() in db.test.ts omits these required fields. Consider creating a narrower type for the SQLite layer.

2. No tests for core heartbeat orchestration (heartbeat.ts:main, runHeartbeat, processProject, gitCommitAndPush, tryPush): These are the most critical business-logic functions in the system and have zero test coverage.

### MEDIUM (4)

1. Shell injection via bash -c in cmd-daemon.ts:139,157: The cron install/uninstall functions pass a path through bash -c, re-introducing shell interpretation.

2. TOML string injection in config.ts:82,91-92: Path and name values are interpolated into TOML without escaping quotes or backslashes.

3. Launchd plist XML injection in cmd-daemon.ts:196-217: Path values interpolated into XML without escaping.

4. No tests for CLI command handlers (cmdInit, cmdImport, cmdDiscover, cmdUpgrade, cmdLocale, cmdRecall): None of the 6 main CLI command wrappers have test files.

### LOW (4)

1. Path traversal in resolveTemplateDir (scaffold.ts:105): Unsanitized locale value used in path construction.

2. Duplicate timestamp utility (alert.ts:54): utcTimestamp() duplicates normalizeTimestamp(new Date()) from common.ts.

3. No test for corrupt SQLite file handling in db.ts.

4. Lock file TOCTOU: Correctly mitigated by O_EXCL, documented for completeness.
